# 文档 [164] Knight
- 类别：characters
- 标识：knight
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Knight
## Overview

The Knight is the silent, genderless protagonist of *Hollow Knight*. It is a child of the Pale King and the White Lady, born in the Abyss with Void inside its shell. Hornet is the Knight's half-sister through their shared father. Like the rest of its Vessel siblings, the Knight is genderless.

The Knight's main weapon is the Nail. It uses Charms, Spells, and Abilities, and draws energy from SOUL.

After climbing out of its birthplace in the Abyss, the Knight witnessed its sibling, the Hollow Knight, being taken out of the Abyss by the Pale King. The entrance to the Abyss was sealed, causing the Knight to fall back down. Sometime after this, despite the entrance being sealed, the Knight and some of its siblings managed to escape the Abyss. Team Cherry has stated that they are not sure how the Knight escaped the Abyss.

Eventually, the Knight ended up wandering outside of Hallownest for unknown reasons. Spending time in this area caused the Knight to lose its memories, but being there did give it a certain resilience.

## Location

The Knight begins the game outside Hallownest and travels throughout the entire kingdom. Key locations include:
- The Abyss (its birthplace)
- The Temple of the Black Egg (where it confronts the Hollow Knight and the Radiance)
- Godhome (accessible via the Junk Pit, where it can ascend through Pantheons)

## Interactions

### In-Game Events

At the beginning of the game, the Knight is equipped with only its Old Nail and the ability to heal itself using SOUL. Throughout the game, the Knight gains access to new powers, Items, and Charms to help it through its journey.

After encountering the Dreamers in the Resting Grounds, the Knight acquires the Dream Nail. With this weapon, it can break the Seals in the Temple of the Black Egg by killing each of the three Dreamers. This allows it to enter the Black Egg, where it can fight the Hollow Knight.

- If the Hollow Knight is faced before obtaining the Void Heart Charm, the Knight kills its sibling and takes its place in sealing the Radiance.
- If the Knight has fought Hornet twice and has the King's Brand and the Shade Cloak, it has access to both halves of the Kingsoul. When the complete Kingsoul is equipped, the Knight can transform this Charm into Void Heart by going to its birthplace at the bottom of the Abyss and remembering its past.
- With Void Heart, the Knight can use the Dream Nail on the Hollow Knight after Hornet holds it down. If the Dream Nail is not used, the Knight has to kill the Hollow Knight. This gives a similar ending as the ending without having Void Heart, but instead, Hornet becomes a Dreamer, her face appearing on the entrance to the Black Egg.
- Using the Dream Nail initiates the fight with the Radiance. At the end of this fight, the Knight breaks its own shell and lands the finishing blows on the Radiance in its Shade form, with the help of the Shade of the Hollow Knight. Both siblings and all the other Shades in the Abyss then return to the Void.

In Godhome, the Knight can ascend by attuning all the Gods of Hallownest and defeating them in the Pantheons. In the Pantheon of Hallownest, at the end of the fight with Absolute Radiance, the Knight breaks its shell and its Shade falls into the Void. The Void Entity then appears, killing Absolute Radiance, after which Void starts leaking from the Godseeker's body in the Junk Pit and eventually bursts out of her. If Godseeker was given a Delicate Flower, the Void and Godseeker disappear instead.

### Health and SOUL

**Health** is represented as Masks, shown in the upper-left corner of the screen. The Knight starts the game with 5 Masks, and can obtain more by collecting Mask Shards. 4 Mask Shards make one new Mask of health, up to a max of 9 total Masks of health. Health is lost by taking damage, either from enemies or from environmental hazards. Health can be regained by resting at a Bench or Hot Spring, by Focusing, or by obtaining a Mask.

**Lifeblood masks**, granted by Lifeseeds and certain Charms, are temporary Masks that cannot be healed using Focus. Lifeblood Masks disappear upon resting at a bench, whereas those granted by Charms regenerate.

**Shade**: When Masks are depleted to 0, the Knight's shell shatters which releases its Shade. After the screen fades back in from black, the Knight is back on the Bench that was last rested on with a third of its SOUL gauge missing and without any Geo. Returning to the area where the Knight died and defeating its Shade restores the lost SOUL gauge and recovers the Geo that was lost. However, if its masks have been depleted to zero without first defeating its Shade, its previously lost Geo cannot be recovered.

**SOUL** is represented as a circular face to the left of the health indicator. SOUL is used to cast Spells, including Focus. Striking enemies with the Nail is the primary source of regaining SOUL, though other tools and objects also grant SOUL. Collecting three Vessel Fragments increases the maximum SOUL by 33.

### Upgrades and Equipment

**Nail**: The Knight's main weapon, able to swing in any direction. The Nail can be swung downwards while the Knight is above spikes, enemies, or certain objects, which can be a useful tool for traversing Hallownest. The Nail can be upgraded for stronger strikes, and charged attacks called Nail Arts can be learned from the Nailmasters.

**Charms**: Special trinkets acquired through adventuring or by purchasing from other bugs. By equipping them on available Notches, Charms enhance the Knight's power through a variety of different methods, including increasing health, reducing heal times, spawning allied hatchlings, and more.

**Spells**: First acquired from the Snail Shaman, these magical attacks deal large amounts of damage in short bursts, at the cost of SOUL. Each Spell can be upgraded to a stronger version by finding hidden rooms throughout Hallownest.

**Abilities**: Skills and tools found throughout Hallownest that allow the Knight to more effectively traverse the terrain and engage enemies in combat, including dashing, wall-jumping, Super-dashing, and double-jumping.

### Hollow Knight: Silksong

In *Hollow Knight: Silksong*, the Knight appears before Hornet during the true ending, Sister of the Void. After the power of the Everbloom fails, Hornet and Lace are saved from being claimed by the tendrils of the Void by the Knight, who attacks the tendrils in retaliation. When Hornet awakes to find their sibling leading the army of the countless fallen Vessels having returned to the Void, she sees glimpses of their ascended collective form, the Void Given Focus. She loses consciousness once more, but her sibling uses multiple tendrils of the Void to lift her and Lace out of the Abyss and back onto the dry land below Pharloom, where the webs of the Abyss have started to fade away from the greater kingdom above. After that, the Vessels once more return to the Abyss.

## Lore

The Knight is a Vessel, one of many children of the Pale King and the White Lady, born in the Abyss with Void inside its shell. It witnessed the Hollow Knight being taken by the Pale King, and after the Abyss was sealed, it fell back down. Despite the seal, the Knight and some siblings escaped. It wandered outside Hallownest, losing its memories but gaining resilience.

The Knight's journey through Hallownest involves collecting the Dream Nail, defeating the Dreamers, and ultimately confronting the Hollow Knight and the Radiance. Depending on the player's actions, the Knight may either take the Hollow Knight's place, defeat the Radiance with the help of the Void, or ascend to godhood in Godhome.

## Trivia

- The Knight's design is taken from Team Cherry's first game, *Hungry Knight*, which was made during a Game Jam that started the company.
- While the two games are very different, Team Cherry has stated that they "liked the main character and the general aesthetic so much that [they] fleshed it out and expanded on it."
- This plan was put forward through the conceptual "Hungry Bug" artworks done by Ari Gibson, which helped visualise and shape the world of *Hollow Knight*.
- Mister Mushroom makes a reference to *Hungry Knight* in his first dialogue with it, saying: *"...It's nice that you were able to help your friend. So you're not hungry any more?"*
- When the Knight has one Mask left, the screen becomes bordered by black lines and Void particles can be seen floating off the Knight. Its posture also changes from upright to a bent over, gasping stance. This posture is removed if the Fury of the Fallen Charm is equipped.
- The Steam Trading Card refers to the Knight as "Hollow Knight".
- The Knight has many nicknames used by various characters, notably:
  - "Little Ghost" by Hornet.
  - "(Little) Traveller" by Elderbug, Oro, and the Nailsmith.
  - "(Little) Wanderer" by numerous other characters such as Bretta and Relic Seeker Lemm.
  - "Lord of Shades" by Shade Beast.
---

# 文档 [166] Last Stag
- 类别：characters
- 标识：last_stag
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Last Stag
## Overview

**The Last Stag** is an NPC in *Hollow Knight* serving as transport across Hallownest. He is a large stag beetle and the last of his kind in Hallownest.

## Location

The Last Stag can be found at any Stag Station that has been unlocked by the Knight. He appears when summoned by ringing the station's bell.

## Interactions

The Last Stag can transport the Knight for free to and from any unlocked Stations. He urges the Knight to open any more Stations they may come across, as it may help him remember the location of the Stag Nest.

At every station, he can tell the Knight more about its surrounding areas, providing a lot of information about the past of the kingdom and its inhabitants. However, he mentions that he was not aware of the existence of the station in the Distant Village and the Hidden Station in the Palace Grounds.

After finding all available Stations, the Last Stag remembers the location of the Stag Nest and can provide a ride to it. Inside, many Stag corpses are found along with a broken egg and a Vessel Fragment. The Last Stag senses that more of his kind might be alive, which rejoices him. His name is then changed to **Old Stag**.

## Lore

Even though his own kind disappeared and old age starts impairing him, the Last Stag remains faithful to his duties. He transports any bug calling him with the bell of a Station, wherever they are. However, his memory has been lacking and he forgot where the Stations are located on the Stagways, even the Stag Nest. Yet, the Last Stag keeps a good memory of the places he once visited and still remembers much of Hallownest's golden age.

His dedication to the Stagways makes him dislike the Tramways the Pale King was building before the latter's disappearance. He also makes no difference between his riders, despite his own feelings about them.

## Trivia

- The *Hollow Knight Beta* contains cut sleeping sprites for the Last Stag. This animation was never implemented in the beta or the final game. The sprites were still present in the release version but were removed in later versions.
- One of the sprites was re-used for a Stag corpse in the Stag Nest.
---

# 文档 [170] Lurien the Watcher
- 类别：characters
- 标识：lurien-the-watcher
- 路径：characters/lurien-the-watcher.json

# 角色：Lurien the Watcher
类型：npc
位置：At the top of the Watcher's Spire in the City of Tears.
Bookish, telescope-loving custodian of the capital. One of the three Dreamers sealing the Hollow Knight.
Watched over the City of Tears from his tower. Chose eternal sleep when the Pale King asked, and is guarded by the Watcher Knights even now.
<b>Lurien the Watcher</b> is an NPC in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. He is one of the Dreamers and is involved in the Knight's quest to destroy the Infection.
Lore
Lurien used to watch over the City of Tears from the Watcher's Spire. The Watcher Knights were his guards, and he had various servants such as his butler. At the top of his Spire, Lurien had a large telescope that looks down over the City of Tears, contributing to his title of "The Watcher".
After the Infection appeared, Lurien became part of the Pale King's plan to seal the Radiance away in the Hollow Knight. He volunteered to be a Dreamer out of loyalty to the Pale King and to protect the City of Tears and the kingdom of Hallownest. Lurien and the other Dreamers sealed the entrance to the Black Egg in the Temple of the Black Egg, which put them into an eternal sleep. He and the other Dreamers attempt to lock the Knight in the Dream Realm after the Resting Grounds encounter.
Once the Knight reaches his physical body in the Watcher's Spire after defeating the Watcher Knights, his mind can be entered by using the Dream Nail. He can then be attacked in his Dream after which Focus can be used to break his Seal. His physical body has disappeared when the Knight wakes up.
Location
Lurien's physical body is located in Watcher's Spire in the City of Tears. The Watcher Knights need to be defeated to reach him.
Achievements
Trivia
When Lurien has been killed, all the previously lit candles in his chamber are extinguished after exiting his dream.
There is a hidden room in the Watcher's Spire which contains Lurien's journal. It can be accessed after taking the lift up to Lurien and breaking the third statue.
Early in development Lurien was known as "Lurian, The Whisperer".
Like the rest of the Dreamers, Lurien has numerous unused lines of dialogue which can still be found in the game's files.
When trying to attack Lurien's physical body in the Watcher's Spire, a Seal appears over his body.
Internally, Lurien has a suggestion of a relationship with another character in the game that is never hinted at in any of the visible lore. Team Cherry did not add this to the game because they did not want to reveal too much about some of the Dreamers.

# 角色：Lurien the Watcher
**Lurien the Watcher** is an NPC in *Hollow Knight*. He is one of the Dreamers and is involved in the Knight's quest to destroy the Infection.
Lore
Lurien used to watch over the City of Tears from the Watcher's Spire. The Watcher Knights were his guards, and he had various servants such as his butler. At the top of his Spire, Lurien had a large telescope that looks down over the City of Tears, contributing to his title of "The Watcher".

Lurien and the other Dreamers sealed the entrance to the Black Egg in the Temple of the Black Egg, which put them into an eternal sleep. He and the other Dreamers attempt to lock the Knight in the Dream Realm after the Resting Grounds encounter.
Once the Knight reaches his physical body in the Watcher's Spire after defeating the Watcher Knights, his mind can be entered by using the Dream Nail. He can then be attacked in his Dream after which Focus can be used to break his Seal. His physical body has disappeared when the Knight wakes up.

# 文档 [181] Mister Mushroom
- 类别：characters
- 标识：mr-mushroom
- 路径：characters/mr-mushroom.json

# 角色：Mister Mushroom
类型：npc
位置：Travels between seven hidden rooms across the kingdom — only visible after acquiring Mister Mushroom from a Bardoon hint.
Quiet, gesturing mushroom traveller. Pops up in seven secret spots, miming a phrase for the Knight to interpret.
A free-DLC easter-egg quest tied to the Hidden Dreams update. Tracking him to every location rewards an achievement and a fond goodbye.
<b>Mister Mushroom</b> is a talking mushroom NPC found throughout Hallownest after all three Dreamers have been killed. His babbles can be heard from a distance, guiding the Knight to his location. He is also referred to as the Herald or Master Herald.
In-game events
Finding him in all seven locations and ending the game rewards the <i>Passing of the Age</i> achievement and a secret cutscene after beating the game.
To talk to him, he must first be hit with the Nail so that he turns around (other damage does not affect him). To understand what he says, the Spore Shroom Charm must be equipped, otherwise, he speaks gibberish and does not move to the next location. However, his Dream Nail dialogue is not gibberish, even without Spore Shroom.
Throughout his dialogue, it is apparent that Mister Mushroom does not acknowledge the Knight and instead seems to be talking to someone else or talking to himself. In the final encounter, he finally acknowledges the presence of the Knight and realizes they have been following him throughout his travels.
Riddle Tablet
The Riddle Tablet is a glowing glyph in a secret room at the bottom right corner of Kingdom's Edge. The hidden opening leading to it is on the right side of one of the vertical shafts above the giant geo deposit in the special room with said deposit. When it is read with the Spore Shroom Charm equipped, the tablet reveals a poem, which gives hints to the locations where Mister Mushroom can be found:
<i>We speak the path of the Master Herald, he who would signal an Age's end.</i>
<i>Spawn of self, their minds unite,</i> (Fungal Wastes)
<i>Aside the source of acid blight,</i> (Kingdom's Edge, near the tram and Isma's Grove)
<i>Aglow in darkest, winding depths,</i> (Deepnest, near Galien)
<i>Winds all howl above fossilstone steps,</i> (Howling Cliffs, in Mato's hut)
<i>Monarchflys in air set still,</i> (Ancient Basin, near the Monarch Wings location)
<i>To Root's domain and snail once shrill,</i> (Fog Canyon, near Overgrown Mound)
<i>Path of Wyrm, at new lands entered,</i> (King's Pass)
<i>There journeys end. The kingdom ventured.</i>
Locations
He can be found in 7 different locations. Each one must be visited in the order described on the Riddle Tablet in order for him to progress to the next location.
Achievements
Trivia
Mister Mushroom is one of the few NPCs who can be "hit" with the Nail without taking damage.
Mister Mushroom was originally created to fill up the empty room where Cornifer used to be in the Fungal Wastes.
Mister Mushroom's first dialogue is a likely reference to Team Cherry's entry 'Hungry Knight' for the Ludum Dare Game Jam 27, in which they first used the character that became the Knight. In the game, the player has to keep feeding on cherries dropped by enemies and kill three bosses (whose icons looks similar to Monomon's) to resurrect a friend.
Once Mister Mushroom leaves after listening to him, the spot he used to be at can still be nail-bounced on and the Dream Nail can still be used which activates his Dream Nail dialogue. This works in every area he appears except for King's Pass until leaving the room and re-entering.
The <i>Passing of the Age</i> achievement is the only one in the game without a monochrome colour palette, instead featuring Mister Mushroom in full-colour.
Mister Mushroom is the only character to appear as an NPC in both Hollow Knight and Hollow Knight: Silksong.

# 文档 [183] Monomon the Teacher
- 类别：characters
- 标识：monomon-the-teacher
- 路径：characters/monomon-the-teacher.json

# 角色：Monomon the Teacher
类型：npc
位置：Suspended in stasis at the heart of the Teacher's Archives, deep in Fog Canyon.
Brilliant jellyfish scholar and one of the three Dreamers binding the Hollow Knight's seal.
Monomon volunteered to dream eternally to help imprison the Radiance. Her seal must be broken to reach the true ending. Her old assistant, Quirrel, returns to be near her one last time.
<b>Monomon the Teacher</b> is an NPC in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. She is one of the Dreamers and is involved in the Knight's quest to destroy the Infection.
Lore
Monomon used to be a chief researcher and teacher of Hallownest. Her archives in Fog Canyon contain strange, jumbled Lore Tablets that contain certain phrases such as:
"KINGLIGHT" and "OLDLIGHT", which are probably the Pale King and the Radiance.
"VESSEL" and "VOID", which are the Vessels and the Void.
"SEAL", "EGG", and "DREAMER", which seem to explain how the Radiance is sealed.
The archives also contain a tank full of Charged Lumaflies, presumably there in order to study them. Monomon is hinted to have sourced the creatures resembling jellyfish found in Fog Canyon, if not only by accident.
When the Infection appeared, Monomon took part in the Pale King's plan to seal the Radiance away in the Hollow Knight. Monomon became a Dreamer to seal the entrance to the Black Egg in the Temple of the Black Egg, which put her into an eternal sleep.
Quirrel was Monomon's apprentice or assistant. She entrusted him with her mask which serves as additional protection for her once she became a Dreamer. Monomon called Quirrel back to Hallownest to undo this protection after the Hollow Knight weakened. However, she and the other Dreamers still attempt to lock the Knight in the Dream Realm after the Resting Grounds encounter.
Once the Knight and Quirrel reach her physical body in the Teacher's Archives, her mind can be entered by using the Dream Nail. Monomon accepts that this must happen and seems to welcome it. She can then be attacked in her Dream after which Focus can be used to break her Seal. Her physical body has disappeared when the Knight wakes up.
Location
Monomon's physical body can be found in the Teacher's Archives in Fog Canyon. Uumuu needs to be defeated to reach her.
Achievements
Trivia
A cut version of the Elegy for Hallownest which has additional lines can still be found in the game files. Monomon herself also has numerous unused lines of dialogue.
When trying to attack Monomon's physical body in the Teacher's Archives, a Seal appears over her body.
In Team Cherry's previous game, <i>Hungry Knight</i>, there are three masks found on the bosses that look similar to Monomon's.
In the original concepts for the Dreamers, all three Dreamers looked identical; sharing Monomon's mask and having the body shape of Lurien. The identical masks can still be seen on the archways outside the Temple of the Black Egg, and on one of the Hollow Knight promotional posters. The identical bodies can still be found on the Hollow Knight fountain in the City of Tears.
<b>Monomon the Teacher</b> is an NPC in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. She is one of the Dreamers and is involved in the Knight's quest to destroy the Infection.
Lore
Monomon used to be a chief researcher and teacher of Hallownest. Her archives in Fog Canyon contain strange, jumbled Lore Tablets that contain certain phrases such as:
"KINGLIGHT" and "OLDLIGHT", which are probably the Pale King and the Radiance.
"VESSEL" and "VOID", which are the Vessels and the Void.
"SEAL", "EGG", and "DREAMER", which seem to explain how the Radiance is sealed.
The archives also contain a tank full of Charged Lumaflies, presumably there in order to study them. Monomon is hinted to have sourced the creatures resembling jellyfish found in Fog Canyon, if not only by accident.
When the Infection appeared, Monomon took part in the Pale King's plan to seal the Radiance away in the Hollow Knight. Monomon became a Dreamer to seal the entrance to the Black Egg in the Temple of the Black Egg, which put her into an eternal sleep.
Quirrel was Monomon's apprentice or assistant. She entrusted him with her mask which serves as additional protection for her once she became a Dreamer. Monomon called Quirrel back to Hallownest to undo this protection after the Hollow Knight weakened. However, she and the other Dreamers still attempt to lock the Knight in the Dream Realm after the Resting Grounds encounter.
Once the Knight and Quirrel reach her physical body in the Teacher's Archives, her mind can be entered by using the Dream Nail. Monomon accepts that this must happen and seems to welcome it. She can then be attacked in her Dream after which Focus can be used to break her Seal. Her physical body has disappeared when the Knight wakes up.
Location
Monomon's physical body can be found in the Teacher's Archives in Fog Canyon. Uumuu needs to be defeated to reach her.
Achievements
Trivia
A cut version of the Elegy for Hallownest which has additional lines can still be found in the game files. Monomon herself also has numerous unused lines of dialogue.
When trying to attack Monomon's physical body in the Teacher's Archives, a Seal appears over her body.
In Team Cherry's previous game, <i>Hungry Knight</i>, there are three masks found on the bosses that look similar to Monomon's.
In the original concepts for the Dreamers, all three Dreamers looked identical; sharing Monomon's mask and having the body shape of Lurien. The identical masks can still be seen on the archways outside the Temple of the Black Egg, and on one of the Hollow Knight promotional posters. The identical bodies can still be found on the Hollow Knight fountain in the City of Tears.
---

# 文档 [184] Monomon the Teacher
- 类别：characters
- 标识：monomon_the_teacher
- 路径：wiki/Monomon_the_Teacher

# 角色：Monomon the Teacher
**Monomon the Teacher** is an NPC in *Hollow Knight*. She is one of the Dreamers and is involved in the Knight's quest to destroy the Infection.
Lore
Monomon used to be a chief researcher and teacher of Hallownest. Her archives in Fog Canyon contain strange, jumbled Lore Tablets that contain certain phrases such as:
"KINGLIGHT" and "OLDLIGHT", which are probably the Pale King and the Radiance.
"VESSEL" and "VOID", which are the Vessels and the Void.
"SEAL", "EGG", and "DREAMER", which seem to explain how the Radiance is sealed.
The archives also contain a tank full of Charged Lumaflies, presumably there in order to study them. Monomon is hinted to have sourced the creatures resembling jellyfish found in Fog Canyon, if not only by accident.
When the Infection appeared, Monomon took part in the Pale King's plan to seal the Radiance away in the Hollow Knight. Monomon became a Dreamer to seal the entrance to the Black Egg in the Temple of the Black Egg, which put her into an eternal sleep.
Quirrel was Monomon's apprentice or assistant. She entrusted him with her mask which serves as additional protection for her once she became a Dreamer. Monomon called Quirrel back to Hallownest to undo this protection after the Hollow Knight weakened. However, she and the other Dreamers still attempt to lock the Knight in the Dream Realm after the Resting Grounds encounter.
Once the Knight and Quirrel reach her physical body in the Teacher's Archives, her mind can be entered by using the Dream Nail. Monomon accepts that this must happen and seems to welcome it. She can then be attacked in her Dream after which Focus can be used to break her Seal. Her physical body has disappeared when the Knight wakes up.
Location
Monomon's physical body can be found in the Teacher's Archives in Fog Canyon. Uumuu needs to be defeated to reach her.
Achievements
Trivia
A cut version of the Elegy for Hallownest which has additional lines can still be found in the game files. Monomon herself also has numerous unused lines of dialogue.
When trying to attack Monomon's physical body in the Teacher's Archives, a Seal appears over her body.
In Team Cherry's previous game, *Hungry Knight*, there are three masks found on the bosses that look similar to Monomon's.
In the original concepts for the Dreamers, all three Dreamers looked identical; sharing Monomon's mask and having the body shape of Lurien. The identical masks can still be seen on the archways outside the Temple of the Black Egg, and on one of the Hollow Knight promotional posters. The identical bodies can still be found on the Hollow Knight fountain in the City of Tears.
---

# 文档 [194] Nailsmith
- 类别：characters
- 标识：nailsmith
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Nailsmith
## Overview

The **Nailsmith** is a Merchant in *Hollow Knight*. He provides a service to strengthen the Knight's Nail for Geo and Pale Ore. He provides the first Nail refinement for Geo only, after which he requires Pale Ore and Geo to upgrade further (see Nail for prices). Each upgrade demands Geo and the rare Pale Ore. He forges with single-minded devotion. Completing his quest with the Pure Nail leads to a choice — spare him to retire to Sheo's hut, or end him for a Mask Shard.

## Location

The Nailsmith is initially located in the west part of the City of Tears, at the eastern edge of the City of Tears. His forge sits in an isolated hut on the outskirts. Later on, if he is spared, he moves to Sheo's hut in Greenpath.

## Interactions

The Nailsmith can be found at his smithy in the outskirts of the City of Tears, in an isolated hut. At first, he can refine the Old Nail into the Sharpened Nail for a small amount of Geo. After that, he requires both Pale Ore and Geo to upgrade it further, with the price and the number of Pale Ore increasing with each successive upgrade.

After having him forge the Pure Nail, the Nailsmith steps outside and asks the Knight to cut him down. Obliging him sends him plummeting down to the waters below and awards the *Purity* achievement. His corpse can be found in the Junk Pit after completing two Pantheons and speaking to the Godseeker.

When not granting his request to "cut him down" and leaving the area, he can be found with Sheo in his hut in Greenpath. Listening to the Nailsmith awards the *Happy Couple* achievement. These achievements are mutually exclusive on a single save as the game autosaves immediately after killing the Nailsmith.

He then remains in Sheo's hut for the rest of the game, engaging in modelling for Sheo and making wooden figurines together. The achievement name, Happy Couple, implies Sheo and the Nailsmith are in a romantic relationship.

It is also possible to kill the Nailsmith with Spells when he asks.

Upgrading the Nail respawns enemies that normally only respawn after sitting on a Bench.

Hitting the exit from the Nailsmith's shop with a long enough nail range causes the knight to hit something as though it were a wall.

## Lore

The Nailsmith is one of the few bugs that lived through the fall of Hallownest. Driven by his craft and working in seclusion, he barely noticed the world changing around him. Even before that, he hardly paid attention to the Kingdom's Five Great Knights. He spends his time honing his craft, hoping to one day forge a Pure Nail, the apex of his work. There are many nails surrounding his hut.

## Trivia

The Nailsmith's quest to forge the perfect nail was part of a Kickstarter stretch goal at $44,000 which was the addition of four new quests to the game: A Nailsmith's Obsession.

The Nailsmith was first revealed in a Kickstarter update, although that information is no longer canonical:

*"Follow a twisting path from the outskirts of the drowning city. Cross a broken bridge and you'll hear it close, the ring of metal and the roar of flame. A craftsman obsessed.*
*Within his forge the Nailsmith is searching, on an endless quest to create a flawless nail.*
*Past failures pile outside his door, exposed to the rains and left to rust. He spares no thought for imperfect things. Nor does he pause to take notice of the countless beings that take their pick of his refuse.*
*But his neglect has impact. His discarded nails have spread wide through Hallownest, clutched tight in the hands of creatures possessed.*
*Only in the Hollow Knight's broken nail does he at last see true potential. Distant and difficult to achieve, but it is in there, waiting - a blade to be honed beyond all others, to be forged into a form so brilliant it transcends its metal and becomes myth."*

The Nailsmith's voicelines were originally recorded for Relic Seeker Lemm. Matthew 'Leth' Griffin, the voice actor for both of them, had to re-record the lines for Lemm because Team Cherry told him that Lemm is supposed to be annoyed with the Knight. Lemm's old lines were subsequently reused for the Nailsmith.

The Dream Nail dialogue of the corpse of the Ancient Nailsmith found in Kingdom's Edge is also *"...Pure..."*, the same as the Nailsmith's corpse's Dream Nail dialogue.

In the promotional art, the Nailsmith has four legs, but in-game, he only has two.
---

# 文档 [196] Pale King
- 类别：characters
- 标识：pale_king
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Pale King
## Overview

The **Pale King** is an NPC in *Hollow Knight*. He plays a major role in the history of Hallownest. He is a higher being who used to be the monarch of Hallownest, mate to the White Lady, and ruler of the White Palace.

## Lore

The Pale King is an ancient Wyrm who burrowed through mountains and across the wasteland until finally stopping in Kingdom's Edge. Once there, the Wyrm shed its shell and transformed into the Pale King. The pale, broken egg found within the Cast-Off Shell hints at this rebirth. He reduced his form in order to match the bugs of Hallownest.

### The Kingdom of Hallownest

After his transformation, the Pale King expanded the minds of several species of bugs in Hallownest, granting them sapience. The Pale King wanted these bugs to devote themselves to him, and in return, he promised them that the kingdom of Hallownest would last eternally.

The Pale King was often depicted as an imposing, gleaming figure with a fiercely horned crown. He was bright and radiant in visage, with the Delicate Flower's pure aura being no match for his light.

Although he was an elusive, reclusive figure who was rarely seen outside his Palace, the Pale King was deified by his citizens. The bugs of Hallownest believed that he created their world and everything in it. Worship was offered through King's Idols. Even the Moth Tribe turned their backs on their creator, the Radiance, and started worshipping the Pale King instead. The Pale King's ability of foresight, the ability to see the future to some extent, caused the mushrooms of Fungal Wastes to accept his rule as well.

He was responsible for much of the architecture found throughout Hallownest, most of it bearing a Hallownest Seal. He also built the Stagways and the Trams.

### The Infection

When the Radiance tried to be remembered again after being almost entirely forgotten, she ended up causing the Infection. To combat this, the Pale King came up with the idea to use a Vessel to seal her away. These Vessels are the children of him and the White Lady, born in the Abyss with Void inside of them.

Three bugs were asked to become Dreamers to form seals on the Temple of the Black Egg which would contain this Vessel. One of them, Herrah, only accepted his proposal if the Pale King had a dalliance with her which would result in a child; this child ended up being Hornet.

Nevertheless, the chosen Vessel, the Hollow Knight, was unable to contain the Infection for eternity due to their purity being misjudged. The Pale King raised the Hollow Knight and formed a bond with them, which may have resulted in their "tarnishing".

At a certain point, after the Infection reappeared, the Pale King and the White Palace disappeared.

## Location

The White Palace can be accessed in the dream realm after the Awoken Dream Nail is used on the corpse of a Kingsmould in the Palace Grounds. The Pale King's corpse can be found on his throne in the throne room.

In the Pantheon of Hallownest, the Pale King's throne room appears after Nightmare King Grimm and before Pure Vessel.

## Interactions

When the Pale King's corpse is struck, it falls off the throne and his half of the Kingsoul Charm drops on the ground.

The Pale King also appears in a memory of the Knight. He can be seen walking out of the Abyss together with the Hollow Knight, after which he seals the door.

The Godseeker observes that although the King was strong, he was completely erased.

## Trivia

- Upon taking the half of the Kingsoul in the White Palace and returning, the Pale King's corpse can no longer be found.
- In an early version of the game, the Gruz Mother fight area contained three statues: one showing the Pale King, the second showing the White Lady and the third, a broken one, potentially representing the Hollow Knight. These statues can also be seen in the top left corner of one of the early maps.
- A silhouette of the Pale King can be seen in the background of White Defender's arena. This is the only place the Pale King can be seen with wings.
---

# 文档 [198] Quirrel
- 类别：characters
- 标识：quirrel
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Quirrel
## Overview

**Quirrel** is an inquisitive, upbeat explorer, fascinated by the myths of Hallownest for reasons he cannot explain. While he remains a simple observer, he is wise of the land's dangers and has some skill with a nail. He is a soft-spoken pilgrim with a clear nail and an easy smile. He crosses paths with the Knight throughout the kingdom.

Once Monomon the Teacher's assistant, Quirrel was entrusted with Monomon's mask when she became a Dreamer. This mask was part of an additional protection enacted upon herself. Quirrel can be seen wearing this mask on top of his head. In the official comic, it is shown that Quirrel ended up outside of Hallownest.

Quirrel lost much of his memory eventually. He was called back to Hallownest by Monomon in order to reverse the protection placed on her. After waking the Knight, he travels Hallownest revisiting the places he forgot, finally resting at the Blue Lake.

## Location

Quirrel can be found in several locations across Hallownest. However, he does not appear in all of them after he is encountered in Fog Canyon. His appearances occur in the following areas:

- Temple of the Black Egg
- Lake of Unn (Crossroads)
- Queen's Station
- Mantis Village
- City of Tears
- Crystal Peak
- Outside the Teacher's Archives (Fog Canyon)
- Before Monomon (Teacher's Archives)
- Blue Lake

## Interactions

### Temple of the Black Egg
Quirrel is first met staring at the Black Egg in wonder. He briefly talks about how he feels drawn to Hallownest. He is aware that both the Knight and himself are ill-equipped for this perilous journey. He explains that many travellers have come down into the ruins and fallen, and lightly suggests that they may have useful belongings that the Knight could use. He leaves if the Knight enters the room west of the False Knight.

### Lake of Unn
Quirrel is found sitting on a rock next to the Bench inside the structure, polishing his nail. He tells the Knight that their Nail is looking a little worn and that they may not fare as well below the surface. He leaves if the Knight acquires the Mantis Claw.

### Queen's Station
Inside the station, Quirrel can be found sitting on the edge of a platform above the entrance to the Stagway. He comments on the activity such place must have had during the kingdom's peak. He leaves if the Knight acquires the Mantis Claw or leaves Queen's Station.

### Mantis Village
If the Knight has entered the deeper part of the Mantis Village where the Mantis Lords can be found, Quirrel can be encountered in the east part of Mantis Village. He hints at seeking out the Nailsmith before proceeding further past the boss fight. He leaves if the Knight defeats the Mantis Lords, enters the City of Tears, enters Deepnest, or listens to him in Mantis Village.

### City of Tears
Quirrel is found sitting on a Bench on the way out of the first building in the City of Tears, looking out the window. He tells the Knight he feels pulled into the city, but is hesitant to enter, not knowing why. He mentions the water coming down endlessly from above and that he wants to see where it comes from before he leaves the Kingdom. He leaves if the Knight listens to him.

### Crystal Peak
Quirrel is found standing next to a huge window at the peak, looking down onto Dirtmouth, pondering. He also comments on the sad fate of the Infected miners relentlessly at their endless task. He leaves if the Knight acquires the Crystal Heart or later encounters him in the City of Tears.

### Outside the Teacher's Archives
Quirrel is found just outside the entrance to the Teacher's Archives, somewhat confused, feeling drawn inside. *After entering this room, he can no longer be found at any of the prior locations in Hallownest.* He later appears during the Uumuu boss fight to help the Knight by puncturing the outer membrane of the boss, allowing the Knight to damage them.

### Before Monomon
After inspecting the tank that Monomon the Teacher is inside, Quirrel jumps up from below. He explains the history of the Teacher and that he played a part in her protection. He holds up his hat, which is revealed to be Monomon's mask, and undoes that protection to help the Knight. After Monomon is killed, he sits there until the Knight leaves. He does not wear Monomon's mask again after this encounter.

### Blue Lake
In the final encounter with Quirrel, he is found sitting next to the Blue Lake, as he said he would want to see where the rainwater is coming from in the City of Tears. He tells the Knight that now, after seeing the world twice over, he finally feels at peace, and he is thankful he could see its beauty again.

After the conversation, the *Witness* achievement is received and the Knight can choose to sit next to him in silence. After leaving the room, Quirrel disappears. His nail can be seen planted into the ground beside the Lake.

## Lore

Quirrel was once Monomon the Teacher's assistant. When Monomon became a Dreamer, she entrusted Quirrel with her mask, which was part of an additional protection enacted upon herself. Quirrel can be seen wearing this mask on top of his head. In the official comic, it is shown that Quirrel ended up outside of Hallownest.

Quirrel lost much of his memory eventually. He was called back to Hallownest by Monomon in order to reverse the protection placed on her. After waking the Knight, he travels Hallownest revisiting the places he forgot, finally resting at the Blue Lake.

## Trivia

- Quirrel's nail can be seen planted into the ground beside the Blue Lake after his final disappearance.
- The *Witness* achievement is awarded after the conversation at the Blue Lake.
- Quirrel does not wear Monomon's mask again after the encounter before Monomon.
- Quirrel is one of the few NPCs who directly assists the Knight in combat, specifically during the Uumuu boss fight.
---

# 文档 [202] Seer
- 类别：characters
- 标识：seer
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Seer
## Overview

The **Seer** is a Quest NPC in *Hollow Knight*. She is a merchant and the mournful elder of the forgotten Moth Tribe. She reads Essence gathered with the Dream Nail and grants relics in return. Slowly fades as the Knight brings her enough Essence. Her parting words — and the End of Pathways achievement — close her arc once 2400 Essence has been delivered.

## Location

The Seer is located in the north part of the Resting Grounds, tucked away inside the Seer's chamber.

## Interactions

The Seer brings the Knight back to her house after they are trapped in the Dream Realm by the Dreamers. She gives the Knight the Dream Nail, which grants access into the dreams of NPCs and enemies along with other abilities. She then urges the Knight to go and collect as much Essence as possible in order to fully awaken the Dream Nail.

When the Knight has collected 2400 Essence and returns to her, she explains more about the history of Hallownest, after which she dissipates into Essence.

### Rewards

- **100 Essence:** Hallownest Seal
- **200 Essence:** Opens the Spirits' Glade
- **300 Essence:** Pale Ore
- **500 Essence:** Dream Wielder Charm
- **700 Essence:** Vessel Fragment
- **900 Essence:** Dreamgate
- **1200 Essence:** Arcane Egg
- **1500 Essence:** Mask Shard
- **1800 Essence:** Awoken Dream Nail and *Awakening* Achievement
- **2400 Essence:** *Ascension* Achievement

## Lore

The Seer is the last surviving member of the Moth Tribe.

## Trivia

- It is implied that the moth spirit who guides the Knight out of the Dream Realm is the Seer, projected into the dream realm through unknown means. She can also fly in this form, though she seems unable to when she is met physically.
- When Seer bursts into Essence during the *Ascension* achievement, a small glowing fly can be seen flying up out of the cloud.
- Seer is one of the few NPCs who is able to detect when they are being Dream Nailed, although rather than acting negatively, she tells the Knight that if they use the Dream Nail on other creatures, hidden things will reveal themselves.
- The journal entry for Nightmare King Grimm is a poem by the Seer.
- In older versions of *Hollow Knight*'s map, the Seer's home is referred to as the "Dream Witch's Hut". In the files, she is also referred to as the "Witch".
- In the original launch version, the Awakening and Ascension achievements appeared to require 1500 and 2600 Essence. They didn't.
---

# 文档 [207] Snail Shaman
- 类别：characters
- 标识：snail-shaman
- 路径：characters/snail-shaman.json

# 角色：Snail Shaman
类型：npc
位置：Inside the Ancestral Mound, beyond the Soul-cracked door.
Last of the Snail Shamans, keeper of soul rituals from before the Pale King's age.
Hands the Knight Howling Wraiths and points the way to the Shaman Stone charm in his crypt below. His clan is also responsible for the Spell Twister and Soul Eater charms.
<b>Snail Shaman</b> is an NPC in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. He gives the Vengeful Spirit Spell to the Knight in the Ancestral Mound.
Lore
Snail Shaman is a member of the snail shaman tribe. His relatives can be found around Hallownest, but since he is bound to the Ancestral Mound he is unable to visit them. He is therefore unaware of their fate.
While Snail Shaman can create Soul Spells such as Vengeful Spirit, he and the other snails are unable to make Spells like Abyss Shriek, having never been to the Abyss.
In-game events
Upon first encounter, the Shaman gifts the Vengeful Spirit Spell to the Knight. Accepting it results in the Knight waking up locked up in a small dungeon, tasked with killing an Elder Baldur within the Ancestral Mound.
The bodies of other snail shamans can be found throughout Hallownest. There is a crystallised one in the Crystallised Mound, one with overgrown flora in the Overgrown Mound and one in the Soul Sanctum that looks like it has been experimented on, as well as a snail sarcophagus where the Soul Eater Charm can be found.
Acquiring Spells from these snails causes Snail Shaman to comment on how these spells remind him of his various relatives.
Location
Snail Shaman is found in the Ancestral Mound in the Forgotten Crossroads. He can be accessed after defeating False Knight or breaking the wall on the left side of False Knight's boss room.
Trivia
Snail Shaman is one of the few NPCs who is able to detect when they are being Dream Nailed.
References
## AREAS

Imposing predator-bug obsessed with cataloguing every creature in Hallownest. Gives the Knight his Journal.
Updates each Hunter's Journal entry as the Knight encounters and slays more creatures. Filling the Journal rewards Hunter's Marks and, eventually, the Mark of Pride charm and a steel-soul-tier completion percentage.

The final living Great Stag of Hallownest. Ferries the Knight between Stag Stations for a small geo fee.
Wakes from a long sleep when the Knight rings the first Stag bell. Each new station added to his network unlocks fast travel and a short memory of the kingdom he once served.

# 文档 [215] Tiktik
- 类别：characters
- 标识：tiktik
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Tiktik
## Overview

**Tiktiks** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are harmless beetles that run from the Knight, using their sharp claws to crawl on floors and ceilings near the surface of the kingdom. They are an easy source of Geo for anyone patient enough to chase them.

## Location

Tiktiks, much like Crawlids, can be found mainly in the northwest of the **Forgotten Crossroads**, as well as in the **Howling Cliffs** and the northeast part of **Greenpath**. One can be found at the top of the **Blue Lake**.

## Interactions

Tiktiks crawl along every surface of the platform they are on, clinging to walls and ceilings, and deal contact damage to the Knight. If knocked off a ledge, they will drop down and continue to crawl along whatever new platform they land on. They do not pursue the Knight. Striking a Tiktik will stun it in place for half a second.

## Lore

In a Kickstarter update, the Tiktik was referred to as **Segmented Clamberbab**, described as: *"A spiky, tenacious little bug that climbs all over the place using its pointed feet. Always seems to be in a bit of a hurry."*

## Trivia

- The Tiktik is one of the few enemies that respawns upon leaving and re-entering the room.
---

# 文档 [216] Tiso
- 类别：characters
- 标识：tiso
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Tiso
## Overview

**Tiso** is a brash wanderer who seeks the Colosseum of Fools for the sake of a challenge. He fights using his tower shield, which he claims conceals a "deadly surprise." He is arrogant, thinking of himself as the ultimate warrior and showing nothing but contempt for the weak. He almost pays no notice to the Knight until later on, and even then he finds them beneath him. Despite his bravado, he is never actually fought. He gives the Knight his shield as a parting gift before entering the Colosseum. He never makes it out — his corpse marks the entrance to the Trial of the Conqueror.

## Location

Tiso can be found in several locations across Hallownest, appearing in a specific sequence:

- **Dirtmouth**: First met by the well after the Mothwing Cloak has been acquired.
- **Queen's Station**: Reappears here after Dirtmouth.
- **Blue Lake**: Seen standing at the western shore, gazing over the water and expressing his dislike for peace and serenity.
- **Colosseum of Fools**: Found sitting on the Bench in the warrior's pit, looking at the ground as if waiting.
- **Kingdom's Edge**: After interacting with him in the Colosseum and completing or failing a Trial, his corpse is found lying on a ledge by the acid pits at the bottom of Kingdom's Edge, dumped with the other slain warriors.
- **Shrine of Believers**: His grave can be found here, labeled "Tiso Spencer" with the words "I know..."

## Interactions

- After the Mothwing Cloak has been acquired, Tiso can be found next to the well in Dirtmouth. He lightly hints at the Colosseum of Fools and expresses his urge to challenge the Knight.
- At the Blue Lake, he stands on the western shore, gazing over the water and expressing his dislike for peace and serenity.
- In the Colosseum of Fools, he sits on the Bench in the warrior's pit, looking at the ground as if waiting. He needs to be interacted with, and then a Trial must be either completed or failed for him to move from his spot on the Bench.
- After this interaction, Tiso's corpse is found lying on a ledge in Kingdom's Edge.
- If Tiso's body is Dream-Nailed, it says: *"...Why?..."*
- Tiso makes a joke appearance with a fake-out boss sequence in the Pantheon of Hallownest before being subsequently crushed by a Brooding Mawlek. This only occurs if he has been listened to in the Colosseum.

## Lore

Tiso is an adventurer who seeks the Colosseum of Fools for the sake of a challenge. He is arrogant, thinking of himself as the ultimate warrior and showing nothing but contempt for the weak. He almost pays no notice to the Knight until later on, and even then he finds them beneath him. Despite his bravado, he is never actually fought. He is killed in the Colosseum of Fools, his body later found dumped by the acid pits at the bottom of Kingdom's Edge with the other slain warriors. His grave can be found in the Shrine of Believers labeled "Tiso Spencer" with the words "I know..." Coincidentally, the Trial of the Fool has a Brooding Mawlek among its creatures, possibly implying that his cause of death was a Brooding Mawlek. Tiso has been confirmed to be killed.

## Trivia

- Tiso is named after Tiso Spencer, the Kickstarter backer who designed him.
- Before release, the shield that Tiso carries was going to be the shell of his fallen comrade. This is never mentioned in the final game.
- According to his original concept art, he would throw his shield like the Marvel superhero Captain America. He also wears his hood to cover his horn-shaped head.
- His concept art also depicted him with a cloak; this isn't seen anywhere through the game.
- If you die during the Trial of the Warrior before getting to the Zote fight and respawn at the bench below the Colosseum, you will see that Zote is still here, but Tiso is missing. This may imply that Zote has somehow managed to kill Tiso.
---

# 文档 [217] Troupe Master Grimm

# 角色：Troupe Master Grimm
类型：npc
位置：Inside the Grimm Troupe's tent, raised in Dirtmouth after lighting the Nightmare Lantern in the Howling Cliffs.
Theatrical, fire-cloaked ringmaster of a travelling troupe that feeds on nightmares. Speaks in flourishes; fights in flames.
Sends the Knight to collect Grimmkin Flames across Hallownest. The ritual ends in either his death and rebirth as the Knight's own Grimmchild — or his banishment, if Brumm's path is followed.

# 文档 [218] Uoma
- 类别：characters
- 标识：uoma
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Uoma
## Overview

**Uomas** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are small gelatinous creatures whose static-charged outer shells give an electric shock on contact. The Uoma is the lesser cousin of the Ooma. It floats lazily across rooms and dies in one strike.

## Location

Uomas are located in almost every room in Fog Canyon, with just a few exceptions.

## Interactions

Uomas float passively in place, dealing damage if the Knight comes into contact with them. When killed, the Uoma's small orange core bounces free. It does not damage the Knight, unlike the Ooma's larger, explosive core.

## Lore

The Uomas are connected in some way to Monomon the Teacher.

## Trivia

- The Uoma is one of the few enemies that respawns upon leaving and re-entering the room.
---

# 文档 [219] Vengefly
- 类别：characters
- 标识：vengefly
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Vengefly
## Overview

**Vengeflies** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are common flying predators across Hallownest, aggressive but fragile — usually a one-shot. They are one of the first and easiest enemies in the game.

## Location

Vengeflies can be found in the following areas:
- Howling Cliffs
- King's Pass
- Forgotten Crossroads
- Greenpath
- City of Tears
- Colosseum of Fools
- Blue Lake

They can also be spawned by the Collector and Vengefly Kings. All but one of the Vengeflies in the Forgotten Crossroads are replaced by **Furious Vengeflies** when it becomes Infected.

## Interactions

Vengeflies hover in the air, moving around a small area. They emit a squawk before homing in on the Knight when they come within range. The recommended tactic is to either wait and strike when it gets within range, or jump and strike down at it. Either way, it will continue to move towards the Knight, making it possible to stay in one place and continue attacking until it is dead.

## Lore

In a Kickstarter update, the Vengefly was referred to as **Vengeward Buzzerfly**:
*"Once this flying predator has caught sight of its prey, it will hunt it relentlessly through the darkness."*

## Trivia

- The Vengefly is one of the few enemies that respawns upon leaving and re-entering the room.
- Vengeflies spawned by the Vengefly King in Greenpath still drop Geo.
---

# 文档 [222] White Lady
- 类别：characters
- 标识：white-lady
- 路径：characters/white-lady.json

# 角色：White Lady
类型：npc
位置：Sealed inside the Queen's overgrown chamber, reachable from the bottom of the gardens through a thorn-blocked passage.
Pale, root-bound queen of Hallownest. Wife of the Pale King and mother of the Vessels and Hornet.
Receiving the Charm of her bound seed (Kingsoul) requires Awoken Dream Nailing both her and the Pale King's broken remains. The fused Kingsoul becomes the Void Heart key to the true ending.
The <b>White Lady</b> is an NPC in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. She gifts one half of the Kingsoul to the Knight in the Queen's Gardens.
Lore
The White Lady is a root higher being who used to be the Queen of Hallownest and the wife of the Pale King. During Hallownest’s prime, the Queen's Gardens were her well-guarded retreat. This area used to belong to the Mosskin, but the White Lady claimed it to create her gardens.
The White Lady is the mother of the Vessels. Out of shame for her part in their creation, she bound herself in the Queen's Gardens to stop herself from having more offspring. Dryya, one of the Five Great Knights, stood guard over her, although Dryya died after defeating numerous Mantis Traitors. The White Lady is not aware of her death.
Over time, the White Lady's vision worsened, and she could not see much anymore. She did sense within her roots the weakening of the Hollow Knight, prompting her to await a visit from a Vessel to give them her part of the Kingsoul.
In-game events
The White Lady is found in the northwest part of the Queen's Gardens inside a cocoon-like dwelling. Outside this structure is the corpse of Dryya.
When the Knight first meets her, she gifts her half of the Kingsoul to them. She then asks the Knight to defeat the Hollow Knight and take their place in sealing the Radiance.
After the Knight has obtained the completed Kingsoul, she comments on their strength and dedication, wondering if they could be more than simply a Vessel. She tells the Knight to visit their birthplace in the Abyss to find out what is at the heart of the Kingsoul.
Location
The White Lady can be found in the northwest part of the Queen's Gardens. This requires defeating the Traitor Lord first.
Trivia
For the White Lady's dialogue where she talks about Hornet, the game still checks whether the King's Brand has been acquired before this dialogue is triggered, even though it is not possible to reach the White Lady without it.
The White Lady is one of the few NPCs who is able to detect when they are being Dream Nailed. However, instead of reacting negatively, she responds with what seems to be hope.
When using any Spell on the White Lady, a Seal appears over her.
In an early version of the game, the Gruz Mother fight area contained three statues: one showing the Pale King, the second showing the White Lady, and the third, a broken one, potentially representing the Hollow Knight. These statues can also be seen in the top left corner of one of the early maps.
A sketch of the White Lady's cocoon depicts it with her head on the front. The in-game cocoon still has this same design including her roots, except the White Lady's face was replaced by the entrance.
The <b>White Lady</b> is an NPC in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. She gifts one half of the Kingsoul to the Knight in the Queen's Gardens.
Lore
The White Lady is a root higher being who used to be the Queen of Hallownest and the wife of the Pale King. During Hallownest’s prime, the Queen's Gardens were her well-guarded retreat. This area used to belong to the Mosskin, but the White Lady claimed it to create her gardens.
The White Lady is the mother of the Vessels. Out of shame for her part in their creation, she bound herself in the Queen's Gardens to stop herself from having more offspring. Dryya, one of the Five Great Knights, stood guard over her, although Dryya died after defeating numerous Mantis Traitors. The White Lady is not aware of her death.
Over time, the White Lady's vision worsened, and she could not see much anymore. She did sense within her roots the weakening of the Hollow Knight, prompting her to await a visit from a Vessel to give them her part of the Kingsoul.
In-game events
The White Lady is found in the northwest part of the Queen's Gardens inside a cocoon-like dwelling. Outside this structure is the corpse of Dryya.
When the Knight first meets her, she gifts her half of the Kingsoul to them. She then asks the Knight to defeat the Hollow Knight and take their place in sealing the Radiance.
After the Knight has obtained the completed Kingsoul, she comments on their strength and dedication, wondering if they could be more than simply a Vessel. She tells the Knight to visit their birthplace in the Abyss to find out what is at the heart of the Kingsoul.
Location
The White Lady can be found in the northwest part of the Queen's Gardens. This requires defeating the Traitor Lord first.
Trivia
For the White Lady's dialogue where she talks about Hornet, the game still checks whether the King's Brand has been acquired before this dialogue is triggered, even though it is not possible to reach the White Lady without it.
The White Lady is one of the few NPCs who is able to detect when they are being Dream Nailed. However, instead of reacting negatively, she responds with what seems to be hope.
When using any Spell on the White Lady, a Seal appears over her.
In an early version of the game, the Gruz Mother fight area contained three statues: one showing the Pale King, the second showing the White Lady, and the third, a broken one, potentially representing the Hollow Knight. These statues can also be seen in the top left corner of one of the early maps.
A sketch of the White Lady's cocoon depicts it with her head on the front. The in-game cocoon still has this same design including her roots, except the White Lady's face was replaced by the entrance.
---

# 文档 [224] Zote
- 类别：characters
- 标识：zote
- 路径：merged

# 角色：Zote
## Overview

**Zote the Mighty** is an NPC in *Hollow Knight*. He is a traveller from outside Hallownest who came to the Kingdom to fulfill a promise, which is ultimately revealed to be a promise of glory for himself. He named his nail "Life Ender" because names supposedly have power. Unfortunately, because it is made of shellwood, it cannot deal damage. While he claims to be the strongest warrior in the land, he is found trapped by weak enemies or claiming the glory of another bug's deeds. He regards the Knight as beneath him and accuses them of constantly getting in his way.

## Location

Zote can be found in several locations across Hallownest after he is saved in Greenpath:

- **Greenpath**: Found along the path leading to Greenpath, held in the mandibles of a Vengefly King.
- **Dirtmouth**: If saved in Greenpath, Zote shows up in Dirtmouth.
- **City of Tears**: Found in a corridor leading back to the storerooms.
- **Deepnest**: Found stuck in spider webs, presumably having been captured by the beasts of Deepnest.
- **Colosseum of Fools**: If saved both times, he is captured and can be found in the resting area.

## Interactions

### Greenpath Encounter
The Knight has the choice to either save him or leave him. If saved, he complains that the Knight got in the way between him and his "prey", introduces himself, and boasts about his supposed mighty deeds. If he is not saved before acquiring the Mantis Claw, he dies in this location, with his nail and shell remaining. Hitting his shell here grants the *Neglect* achievement.

### Dirtmouth
If saved in Greenpath, Zote talks to the Knight in an arrogant fashion.

### City of Tears
Zote has forgotten the Knight and introduces himself again.

### Deepnest
Once again the Knight has the choice to either save him or leave him, though this time leaving him does not result in his death. If saved, he once again complains about the Knight meddling in his supposed heroics.

### Colosseum of Fools
If the Knight saves him both times, he is captured and found in the resting area, where he brags about his skills and how his capture was part of his plan. He then becomes the final boss of the first trial. Contrary to his boasts, as a boss, he is very weak, dealing no damage due to his nail being made of shellwood. When Zote begins his battle, the audience laughs at him.

### Bretta
Bretta falls for him; her drawings and dolls of the Knight are replaced by a single portrait of Zote. Here he recites "The Fifty Seven Precepts Of Zote". In the basement of Bretta's house, the dream boss version of Zote, Grey Prince Zote, can be fought. Defeating Grey Prince Zote at least once leads to Bretta being skeptical about his "heroic" adventure, and defeating it 4 more times leads to Bretta leaving the spot, because she is certain his "heroic" adventure is fake.

### Hall of Gods
While Zote alone is too weak a creature to partake in the Godseeker's ritual, he is still present in other forms in the Hall of Gods. Grey Prince Zote appears in the Pantheon of the Sage and the Hall of Gods. Additionally, in the Hall of Gods is found an endless gauntlet called The Eternal Ordeal which is an infinite number of dangerous Zotelings of various types. Zote's statue is also present in the Hall of Gods.

## Lore

Zote is a traveller from outside Hallownest who came to the Kingdom to fulfill a promise. This is ultimately revealed to be a promise of glory for himself. He named his nail "Life Ender" because names supposedly have power. Unfortunately, because it is made of shellwood, it cannot deal damage. While he claims to be the strongest warrior in the land, he is found trapped by weak enemies or claiming the glory of another bug's deeds. He regards the Knight as beneath him and accuses them of constantly getting in his way.

## Trivia

- Zote was the first character revealed in a Kickstarter update:
  > "Times are hard for Dirtmouth, the small town built above the ruined underground kingdom of Hallownest. The townsfolk are slowly disappearing; savage creatures prowl beneath the surface and a strange poison in the earth refuses to let any vegetation grow. But lo! From the mists a proud figure emerges, ready to defeat the formless evil that plagues the populace. With his sword held aloft and a fiery determination to protect the helpless, this giant of bugkind strides confidently into the light and..."
  > "Oh, it's Zote. False alarm everybody."
  > "Zote, self-proclaimed 'Knight of the People', recently turned up in Dirtmouth and started demanding free lodgings, food and attention from the townsfolk. Claiming to be a rival of the Hollow Knight and his superior in every way, Zote has supposedly come to Dirtmouth to defeat the evil creatures lurking in the depths and find the source of the poison."
  > "When he isn't having one of his frequent rest stops in town, Zote will be exploring the depths of Hallownest with his unique, home-made nail in hand. He favours caution and patience above all else, so he doesn't always make the same kind of progress as the Hollow Knight. Nor does he have the same successes due to what he calls his 'atrocious, appallingly unfair bad luck'."
  > "If you see him during your travels, Zote will be more than happy to stop and chat, pointing out everything you've been doing wrong during your adventure so you can learn from his example."

- One of the Kickstarter goals was for Zote to become a playable character, but that goal was not reached.
- A charm called "Zote Charm" was an idea that never made it into the game. It would have made the Knight die in one hit.
- Code exists within the game that causes Zote to die while in Deepnest, though achieving this state is impossible without the use of mods.
- Zote has an unconfirmed game titled "Hollow Knight: ZoteBoat".
---

# 文档 [227] Dashmaster
- 类别：charms
- 标识：dashmaster
- 路径：merged

# 护符：Dashmaster
## Overview

**Dashmaster** is a Charm in *Hollow Knight*. It decreases the cooldown of the Mothwing Cloak and allows the Knight to dash downwards. Essential for speedruns and precision platforming.

## Effect

- Shortens dash cooldown from 0.6 to 0.4 seconds.
- Unlocks a vertical down-dash.
- When wearing this Charm, it is possible to use the Shade Cloak to dash downwards.
- Dashing downwards prevents the Knight from staggering when falling from great heights.
- With the downwards dash, it is possible to use a Dash Slash, however the Dash Slash will still be oriented horizontally.

## Location

Royal Waterways — behind a hidden wall near the dung pool, requires Mantis Claw to reach.

## Notch Cost

2 Notches

## Synergies

- **Sharp Shadow**: No specific synergy details provided beyond the charm name being listed as a synergy.
- **Sprintmaster**: Further increases the movement speed bonus to 39%.

## Trivia

- When the Dashmaster's statue is struck with the Dream Nail, it gives the lines:  
  *"...Dash faster... Dash further... Dash forever..."*
---

# 文档 [241] Grubsong
- 类别：charms
- 标识：grubsong
- 路径：merged

# 护符：Grubsong
## Overview

**Grubsong** is a Charm in *Hollow Knight*. It causes the Knight to gain SOUL each time they take damage. The charm is a reward from the Grubfather for rescuing 10 Grubs across Hallownest. It trivializes Focus-based survival when paired with Quick Focus.

## Effect

When the Knight takes damage, Grubsong grants 15 SOUL (out of the 33 needed to heal). The amount of Mask damage taken in one hit does not impact the amount of SOUL gained — it always grants 15 SOUL. This provides a good amount of SOUL to use as healing in compensation for taking damage. The SOUL provided per hit is not enough for a heal on its own, but combined with SOUL gathered by striking enemies or with other Charms that help gather SOUL faster, this Charm becomes incredibly useful for a Spell-focused build. It also shines in difficult platforming areas where enemies are not readily available for gathering SOUL.

*(注：另一来源称获得10 SOUL per mask of damage taken)*

## Location

Gifted by the Grubfather after 10 Grubs have been freed across Hallownest.

## Notch Cost

1 Notch.

## Synergies

- **Grubberfly's Elegy**: Increases the SOUL gained from Grubsong to 25 per hit (instead of 15).
- **Quick Focus**: Pairs well with Grubsong to make Focus-based survival much easier.
- **Joni's Blessing**: Listed as a synergy charm (effect not detailed in sources).

## Trivia

- The amount of Mask damage taken in one hit does not impact the amount of SOUL gained; it always grants 15 SOUL (25 with Grubberfly's Elegy).
---

# 文档 [249] Mark of Pride
- 类别：charms
- 标识：mark-of-pride
- 路径：charms/mark-of-pride.json

# 护符：Mark of Pride
+25% nail range, the largest single-charm reach buff. Stacks additively with Longnail.
效果：Increases the range of the Knight's nail even further.
槽位消耗：3
获取位置：Mantis Village — earned by defeating the Mantis Lords and being honored by the tribe.
联动：longnail（护符名称）
联动：grubberflys-elegy（护符名称）
联动：quick-slash（护符名称）
<b>Mark of Pride</b> is a Charm in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It increases the range of the Nail by 25%.
Usefulness
It is useful for keeping distance from more dangerous enemies and for performing safer Nail-bounces.
While it grants a longer range than the Longnail Charm, it is more challenging to acquire and has higher Notch cost.
The range of both Nail Arts and the beam from the Grubberfly's Elegy Charm are unaffected by Mark of Pride.
How to Acquire
In the Mantis Village, in a chest in a room northeast of the Mantis Lords arena. This room can only be accessed after defeating the Mantis Lords.
Charm Synergies
Charm Combo Tips
Notes

# 文档 [253] Quick Slash
- 类别：charms
- 标识：quick-slash
- 路径：charms/quick-slash.json

# 护符：Quick Slash
Reduces the nail swing cooldown by ~0.25s, increasing damage-per-second by roughly 70%. The single strongest melee charm.
效果：Strike with the nail much more rapidly.
槽位消耗：3
获取位置：Kingdom's Edge — in a hidden room above the Whispering Root, accessible after Mantis Claw + Monarch Wings.
联动：fragile-strength（护符名称）
联动：mark-of-pride（护符名称）
联动：longnail（护符名称）
<b>Quick Slash</b> is a Charm in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It allows for more rapid Nail strikes.
Usefulness
Quick Slash can increase total damage output while slashing with the Nail. This Charm is more effective than Fragile Strength/ Unbreakable Strength in most situations, as it not only increases the rate at which the Nail deals damage but also how quickly it accumulates SOUL.
How to Acquire
Located in Kingdom's Edge, on a massive anvil in a hidden room in front of a massive corpse known as an "Ancient Nailsmith".
Finding it requires travelling to the very east end of Kingdom's Edge past Oro's hut and locating a breakable floor next to his training dummy. After traversing down a few levels, and looping up the west end of the section, there is a small tunnel located within a wall leading to the Charm.
Note that there is spike-filled room with a Great Hopper. The Great Hopper makes it immensely difficult to cross through the spikes.
Take out any primal aspids before entering this room or else they will make things even more tough.
Charm Combo Tips
Trivia
When using the Dream Nail on the Ancient Nailsmith it yields the line <i>" ...Pure... "</i>.
This is the same Dream Nail dialogue of the corpse of the Nailsmith found in the Junk Pit.
Notes
References

# 文档 [258] Sharp Shadow
- 类别：charms
- 标识：sharp-shadow
- 路径：charms/sharp-shadow.json

# 护符：Sharp Shadow
The Shade Cloak now damages enemies it passes through and lasts slightly longer. Combine with Dashmaster for a near-constant dash.
效果：Shade Cloak dashes deal damage and travel further.
槽位消耗：2
获取位置：Deepnest — behind a fragile wall in the Failed Tramway, reached via Shade Cloak.
联动：dashmaster（护符名称）
联动：sprintmaster（护符名称）
<b>Sharp Shadow</b> is a Charm in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It damages enemies when dashing through them and increases dash length when using the Shade Cloak.
}}
Trivia
When using the Shade Cloak with Sharp Shadow the Knight turns into a six-eyed void creature for a split second before reverting back to normal.
The pedestal on which the Sharp Shadow Charm is found resembles an empty Soul Totem covered with twisted black vines of what is possibly Void.
Shadow Dashing through an Ooma while using Sharp Shadow causes its explosive core to always go to the right, independently of the direction the Knight dashes. This effect is also present in the bodies of enemies killed by the Shadow Dash (though its much easier to see in flying enemies). Whether this is intentional or a bug in the in-game physics is unknown.
When using the  Nail Binding in any  Pantheon, Sharp Shadow's damage is not affected. Its damage is also not affected by the Fragile Strength/ Unbreakable Strength and Fury of the Fallen Charms.
Notes

# 护符：Sharp Shadow
**Sharp Shadow** is a Charm in *Hollow Knight*. It damages enemies when dashing through them and increases dash length when using the Shade Cloak.
}}
Trivia
When using the Shade Cloak with Sharp Shadow the Knight turns into a six-eyed void creature for a split second before reverting back to normal.
The pedestal on which the Sharp Shadow Charm is found resembles an empty Soul Totem covered with twisted black vines of what is possibly Void.
Shadow Dashing through an Ooma while using Sharp Shadow causes its explosive core to always go to the right, independently of the direction the Knight dashes. This effect is also present in the bodies of enemies killed by the Shadow Dash (though its much easier to see in flying enemies). Whether this is intentional or a bug in the in-game physics is unknown.
When using the  Nail Binding in any  Pantheon, Sharp Shadow's damage is not affected. Its damage is also not affected by the Fragile Strength/ Unbreakable Strength and Fury of the Fallen Charms.

# 文档 [262] Spell Twister
- 类别：charms
- 标识：spell-twister
- 路径：charms/spell-twister.json

# 护符：Spell Twister
Each spell costs 24 SOUL instead of 33, letting the Knight cast four spells from a full bar instead of three. Mandatory in caster builds.
效果：Reduces the SOUL cost of casting spells.
槽位消耗：2
获取位置：Atop the Soul Sanctum tower, accessible after defeating the Soul Master.
联动：shaman-stone（护符名称）
联动：soul-eater（护符名称）
<b>Spell Twister</b> is a Charm in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It reduces the amount of SOUL required to cast Spells. Focus is exempt from this.
Usefulness
This Charm stacks well with Charms that generate SOUL, like Soul Catcher or Grubsong, as it uses SOUL more efficiently instead of generating it. It is also much more efficient than Soul Catcher in terms of Nail hits per Spell; of course, this comes at the drawback of not being able to use this added efficiency on Focus.
This Charm can also be used in some advanced skips as it lets the Knight use 4 Spells in a short time instead of only 3.
How to Acquire
A secret room on the top of the Soul Sanctum, just before fighting Soul Master. The room which leads up to it is filled with Mistakes and Follies which can make reaching the Charm nearly impossible without taking damage as these enemies may spawn right onto the Knight.
The Charm itself is found attached to some sort of machine similar to the Lore Tablets found around the area.
Charm Combo Tips
<b>Spell Twister</b> is a Charm in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It reduces the amount of SOUL required to cast Spells. Focus is exempt from this.
Usefulness
This Charm stacks well with Charms that generate SOUL, like Soul Catcher or Grubsong, as it uses SOUL more efficiently instead of generating it. This Charm can also be used in some advanced skips as it lets the Knight use 4 Spells in a short time instead of only 3.
How to Acquire
A secret room on the top of the Soul Sanctum, just before fighting Soul Master. The room which leads up to it is filled with Mistakes and Follies which can make reaching the Charm nearly impossible without taking damage as these enemies may spawn right onto the Knight.
The Charm itself is found attached to some sort of machine similar to the Lore Tablets found around the area.
Charm Combo Tips
---

# 文档 [271] Unbreakable Strength
- 类别：charms
- 标识：unbreakable-strength
- 路径：charms/unbreakable-strength.json

# 护符：Unbreakable Strength
Permanent version of Fragile Strength. Forged by Divine for an extra 15,000 geo on top of the broken charm.
效果：Increases nail damage by 50%. No longer breaks on death.
槽位消耗：3
获取位置：Divine's tent in Dirtmouth, after the Grimm Troupe arrives.
联动：quick-slash（护符名称）
联动：mark-of-pride（护符名称）
HK Infobox Charm
|label1 = Normal
|image1 = Fragile Strength.png
|description1 =
|effect1 =
Increases Nail damage by 50%
Breaks upon death
Can be given to Divine to turn it Unbreakable
|notch_cost1 = 3
|title2 = Fragile Strength
|label2 = Broken
|image2 = Broken Strength.png
|description2 =
|effect2 =
Cannot be equipped
Must be repaired by Leg Eater in order to be used again
|notch_cost2 = -1
|title3 = Unbreakable Strength
|label3 = Unbreakable
|image3 = Unbreakable Strength.png
|description3 =
|effect3 = Increases Nail damage by 50%
The downside is that once broken, Leg Eater only repairs it for a price. In the late-game, the cost may not be much of an issue, but the trip to Leg Eater might be. Dreamgate can be used to reach Leg Eater more easily.
This Charm is quite potent, although it breaks upon death. One way to make use of the Charm is to only use it in situations where death is unlikely, such as exploration, or in tandem with survivability-increasing Charms, while also avoiding its use in boss battles, except for Dream Boss battles and  Godhome battles (as the Charm does <b>not</b> break when dying to these bosses).
Lastly, its drawback is negated in Steel Soul runs since the run is over upon death anyway, making Fragile Strength one of the most powerful and useful Charms in a Steel Soul run.
How to Acquire
Purchased from Leg Eater in the Fungal Wastes for . Wearing the Defender's Crest Charm causes Leg Eater to lower the cost to .
Shop description:
<i>You're weak, aren't you? You should give me Geo. If you do, I'll give you this charm I made.
It will make you stronger. Your enemies, and everyone else, will fear you at last...</i>
When broken, Leg Eater can repair it for , or, while wearing the Defender's Crest, for .
Shop description when broken:
<i>It's broken now, and its power is sleeping. Very sad! Give me Geo, and I'll fix it.</i>
Once the Grimm Troupe has been summoned, Divine becomes accessible in Dirtmouth. To get the unbreakable version of Fragile Strength, it must be equipped before listening to her, then it must be given to her when prompted. She eats the Charm, then asks for . Once the Geo is paid, she gives the unbreakable version of Fragile Strength, Unbreakable Strength.
Charm Combo Tips
Notes
