# 文档 [273] Void Heart
- 类别：charms
- 标识：void-heart
- 路径：charms/void-heart.json

# 护符：Void Heart
Replaces the Kingsoul after taking it into the Birthplace at the bottom of the Abyss. Pacifies all Siblings and unlocks the Dream No More ending and the Pantheon of Hallownest.
效果：Unifies the Knight with the void. Cannot be unequipped; enables alternate endings.
获取位置：Birthplace at the bottom of the Abyss, equipped automatically upon entry while wearing the Kingsoul.
Void Heart is a Charm in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It causes Siblings, Void Tendrils, and the Shade to become passive. It also unlocks 4 Endings and allows entry into the  Pantheon of Hallownest.
Usefulness
This charm replaces the Kingsoul Charm and cannot be unequipped. However, it no longer has Kingsoul's effects, nor does it use any Notches.
Having Void Heart unlocks new dialogue with Confessor Jiji, Steel Soul Jinn, the White Lady, Hornet, and Bardoon.
How to Acquire
Found in a secret area at the bottom of the Abyss known as the Birthplace. The area's entrance only opens if the Kingsoul Charm is equipped. At the end of the area is an egg which, upon being hit with the Dream Nail, reveals a memory of the Knight involving Vessels and the Pale King. It is after traversing this memory that the Kingsoul is changed into Void Heart.
Achievements
Trivia
It is not possible to die during the climb up the Abyss after which Void Heart is obtained. Damage can be taken after being hit by spikes, but the Knight's health never runs out.
The Knight also has infinite SOUL during the climb.
Void Heart is the only Charm that does not use up a charm notch and is also the only charm that cannot be regularly unequipped by the Knight.
The only time Void Heart can ever be unequipped is when using the Charm Binding in the Pantheons.
Void Heart is <b>automatically equipped</b> once obtained without the need to sit on a Bench.
When Void Heart is obtained, a distorted version of the normal sound for getting items and abilities is played, similar to obtaining Salubra's Blessing.
While the egg in the Birthplace can be hit with the Dream Nail from either the left or right side, the Dream Nail hitbox is only on the reflective part of the egg.
The egg stops showing a reflection of the Knight after obtaining Void Heart.

# 文档 [275] Wayward Compass
- 类别：charms
- 标识：wayward-compass
- 路径：charms/wayward-compass.json

# 护符：Wayward Compass
Without this charm, the map only shows rooms — not where you are inside them. Often the first charm players buy.
效果：Reveals the Knight's location on the map.
槽位消耗：1
获取位置：Sly's shop in Dirtmouth.
<b>Wayward Compass</b> is a Charm in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It shows the location of the Knight on the Map.
Usefulness
This Charm is useful for exploration and is good during a first playthrough. It is recommended to switch to something more combat-oriented when preparing for a boss battle.
Once a keen knowledge of the map's layout is attained, this Charm is no longer worthwhile.
How to Acquire
Bought from Iselda in Dirtmouth for  after the first encounter with Cornifer.
Shop description:
<i>Highly recommended! If you're having trouble finding your way in the maze of ruins below us, try this charm.
It will pinpoint your location on the map. Incredibly helpful for finding your bearings in unfamiliar locations!</i>
Trivia
The location of the Knight is shown even when no map of the area has been bought.
When the Knight is in the passageway between the City of Tears and the  Junk Pit, Wayward Compass shows them as being below Dirtmouth, on the Map.
Within the code of Hollow Knight Wayward, Compass increases an unknown and useless stat called "Flight Time", which seemingly would increase how long you could fly but it doesn't affect gameplay in any way.
<b>Wayward Compass</b> is a Charm in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It shows the location of the Knight on the Map.
Usefulness
This Charm is useful for exploration and is good during a first playthrough. It is recommended to switch to something more combat-oriented when preparing for a boss battle.

It will pinpoint your location on the map. Incredibly helpful for finding your bearings in unfamiliar locations!</i>

When the Knight is in the passageway between the City of Tears and the  Junk Pit, Wayward Compass shows them as being below Dirtmouth, on the Map.
Within the code of Hollow Knight Wayward, Compass increases an unknown and useless stat called "Flight Time", which seemingly would increase how long you could fly but it doesn't affect gameplay in any way.

# 文档 [276] Wayward Compass
- 类别：charms
- 标识：wayward_compass
- 路径：wiki/Wayward_Compass

# 护符：Wayward Compass
**Wayward Compass** is a Charm in *Hollow Knight*. It shows the location of the Knight on the Map.
Usefulness
This Charm is useful for exploration and is good during a first playthrough. It is recommended to switch to something more combat-oriented when preparing for a boss battle.
Once a keen knowledge of the map's layout is attained, this Charm is no longer worthwhile.
How to Acquire
Bought from Iselda in Dirtmouth for  after the first encounter with Cornifer.
Shop description:
Highly recommended! If you're having trouble finding your way in the maze of ruins below us, try this charm.
It will pinpoint your location on the map. Incredibly helpful for finding your bearings in unfamiliar locations!
Trivia
The location of the Knight is shown even when no map of the area has been bought.
When the Knight is in the passageway between the City of Tears and the  Junk Pit, Wayward Compass shows them as being below Dirtmouth, on the Map.
Within the code of Hollow Knight Wayward, Compass increases an unknown and useless stat called "Flight Time", which seemingly would increase how long you could fly but it doesn't affect gameplay in any way.
---

# 文档 [277] Weaversong

- 标识：weaversong
- 路径：charms/weaversong.json

# 护符：Weaversong
Constantly maintains a trio of weaverling minions. They follow the Knight and deal nominal damage, but distract enemies remarkably well.
效果：Spawns up to three weaverling allies that attack enemies.
槽位消耗：2
获取位置：Weavers' Den, deep in Deepnest.
联动：defenders-crest（护符名称）
联动：grimmchild（护符名称）

# 文档 [280] Crystal Heart
- 类别：skills
- 标识：crystal-heart
- 路径：skills/crystal-heart.json

# 技能/法术：Crystal Heart
类型：movement
Hold the skill button to charge, then release for a long horizontal or vertical super-dash. Required to clear several crystal-walled rooms.
效果：Channel crystal energy to dash across long distances.
获取方式：Found in the deepest chamber of Crystal Peak, past the Crystal Guardian.
所在区域：{'slug': 'crystal-peak', 'name': 'Crystal Peak'}
<b>Crystal Heart</b> is an Ability in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It allows the Knight to fly forward horizontally until colliding with a wall or enemy that is not killed by the dash.
Function
Hold SUPER DASH while on the ground or clinging to a wall to concentrate force. Release the button at full charge to blast forwards and fly through the air. The Knight continues moving forward until interrupted by damage or the environment, by pressing JUMP or by tapping SUPER DASH again.
The Super Dash deals 10 damage on contact with an enemy, and any enemy killed by this hit does not damage the Knight or stop their movement.
How to Acquire
Found in an old mining golem at the end of a platforming segment in Crystal Peak. Requires Mantis Claw.
Trivia
It takes 0.8 seconds to charge the Crystal Heart.
It is possible to use the Dream Nail on the old mining golem, which gives the following dialogue:
<i>"DIG...DIG...CRUSH...DIG...LIFT...DIG...LIFT...DIG...
CRUSH...OBEY...DIG...LIFT...CRUSH...DROP...
DROP...DIG...LIFT...DIG...CRUSH...OBEY...DIG...
DIG...DIG...LIFT...FOLLOW...OBEY...FOLLOW...OBEY...
CRUSH...CRUSH...OBEY...CRUSH...OBEY...CRUSH...
CRUSH...CRUSH...CRUSH...CRUSH...CRUSH...CRUSH..."</i>

# 文档 [284] Desolate Dive
- 类别：skills
- 标识：desolate-dive
- 路径：skills/desolate-dive.json

# 技能/法术：Desolate Dive
类型：spell
Launches the Knight straight down. Damages enemies on impact and produces a shockwave that breaks soul-cracked floors.
效果：Smash downward with a soul-empowered nail blast.
获取方式：Reward for defeating the Soul Master atop the Soul Sanctum.
所在区域：{'slug': 'soul-sanctum', 'name': 'Soul Sanctum'}
<b>Desolate Dive</b> is a Spell in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. Using it strikes the ground with concentrated SOUL, breaking floors and damaging enemies.
Function
Press FOCUS/CAST or QUICK CAST while holding DOWN to cause the Knight to slam into the ground, creating a shockwave that spreads out and up. The dive deals 15 damage, while the shockwave deals 20.
The Knight is invincible for 0.4 seconds during and after using Desolate Dive. This allows for chaining uses of Desolate Dive to avoid enemy damage as long as the Knight has enough SOUL. Using Desolate Dive in quick succession cancels the invincibility frames of the Spell if it is cast while the previous Spell's invincibility frames have not yet run out.
Desolate Dive also allows breaking certain floors, such as those to exit the Soul Sanctum and to enter Crystal Peak.
Modifiers
Shaman Stone increases the damage dealt by Desolate Dive by 51%.
Spell Twister lowers the SOUL cost to cast Desolate Dive to 24 SOUL.
Can be upgraded to Descending Dark.
Damage Values
Charm
Dive Damage
Shockwave Damage
Total Damage
None
15
20
35
Shaman Stone
23
30
53
How to Acquire
Reward for defeating Soul Master in the City of Tears.
Trivia
Desolate Dive was revealed in a Kickstarter update where it was referred to as the <b>Tyrant's Fist</b>:
<i>"This ancient, royal magic allows you to focus energy into your fist and slam it down into the ground, releasing a shockwave that blows away foes and can even rupture the earth you stand on!"</i>
Descending Dark and Desolate Dive can be used while Dung Defender is underground to force him out and stagger him.
After obtaining Desolate Dive, the Knight's SOUL is completely refilled.
References
ZH:荒芜俯冲

# 文档 [285] Dream Gate

- 路径：skills/dream-gate.json

# 技能/法术：Dream Gate
类型：dream
Plant a dream-gate marker anywhere in Hallownest, then warp back from any bench or rest spot. Cuts hours off of late-game backtracking.
效果：Place a portable warp point that the Knight can return to at any time.
获取方式：Purchased from the Seer for 600 dream essence in Spirit's Glade.
所在区域：{'slug': 'spirits-glade', 'name': "Spirit's Glade"}

# 文档 [286] Dream Nail
- 类别：skills
- 标识：dream-nail
- 路径：skills/dream-nail.json

# 技能/法术：Dream Nail
类型：dream
A second nail used to read inner thoughts, harvest dream essence, and open Dream Gates. Drains 33 SOUL per hit on enemies.
效果：Cut through the veil of dreams. Drains SOUL from enemies.
获取方式：Awoken from the Seer's hand in Spirit's Glade.
所在区域：{'slug': 'spirits-glade', 'name': "Spirit's Glade"}
The <b>Dream Nail</b> is an Ability in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It can collect Essence and enter dreams.
Lore
The Dream Nail is a sacred weapon and talisman, which can cut the veil that separates the waking world from dreams. It appears to have been made by the Moth Tribe. The Dream Nail allows its user to not only read the thoughts of an entity, or even inanimate objects, but also enter specific sections of the Dream Realm.
Before the Knight acquires it, the blade dulled over time, making it necessary to fill it with enough Essence to awaken it. Essence are the fragments of light that dreams are composed of. Dreams can also take the shape of those who have passed away. Dreams and memories cling onto the Dream Nail when Essence is collected.
Another one of the Dream Nail's abilities is to teleport the user from one place to another through dreams. The user warps by imagining a great gate to a location connected to them, provided the location has a strong connection to dreams.
Function
Hold down DREAM NAIL to charge and swing the Dream Nail. This can perform several functions:
Extract Essence from Spirits
Activate Whispering Roots
Collect SOUL from living enemies (33 SOUL)
Challenge Warrior Dreams
Read the minds of NPCs, Enemies (excluding Warrior Dreams), and some statues and corpses
Instantly kill both the Shade and Siblings
Summon  The Grimm Troupe
Use to set or travel to a  Dreamgate (Requires 900 Essence)
Enter the Dream Realm
Challenge Dream Bosses
Access the Shrine of Believers
Enter the minds of Dreamers
Access the White Palace (Awoken Dream Nail, requires 1800 Essence)
Access  Godhome
Obtain Void Heart
Challenge the Radiance
Switch boss forms in the  Hall of Gods
The Dream Wielder Charm, granted by the Seer after collecting 500 Essence, greatly reduces the charge time of the Dream Nail and doubles the SOUL gained from hitting living enemies (from 33 to 66).
How to Acquire
The Dream Nail is acquired in the Resting Grounds by inspecting the Dreamers Memorial. Doing so sends the Knight into a dream where they receive the Dream Nail from a Moth.
 Awoken Dream Nail
After collecting 1800 Essence, the Dream Nail can be awoken. This allows access to dreams and memories that were previously hidden. The Awoken Dream Nail can be used on the corpse of the Kingsmould in the Palace Grounds. This grants entry to the White Palace.
Furthermore, the Awoken Dream Nail can be used to view the Dream Nail dialogue of the Shade Cloak creature in the Abyss. This creature has different Dream Nail dialogue depending on whether Void Heart has been obtained.
Essence
Essence is the energy gained from multiple sources after obtaining the Dream Nail. After obtaining certain amounts of Essence, the Knight can return to the Seer for rewards. A total of 2400 is needed for all in-game rewards and achievements, though up to 3208 essence is available from exploration and bosses. Warping using the Dreamgate uses 1 Essence each time.
Essence Sources
Using Dream Nail on a Spirit (26 total)
Collecting Essence spawned by a Whispering Root (482 total)
Defeating a Warrior Dream (1100 total)
Elder Hu (100)
Galien (200)
Gorb (100)
Markoth (250)
Marmu (150)
No Eyes (200)
Xero (100)
Defeating a Dream Boss (1600 total)
Failed Champion (300)
Grey Prince Zote (300)
Lost Kin (400)
White Defender (300)
Soul Tyrant (300)
Regular enemies have a chance to drop Essence:
If less Essence was spent on warping to a Dreamgate than getting randomly from Enemies: 0.33% (1/300)
If more Essence was spent on warping to a Dreamgate than getting randomly from Enemies: 1.67% (1/60)
If Dream Wielder is equipped and less Essence was spent on warping to a Dreamgate than getting randomly from Enemies: 0.5% (1/200)
If Dream Wielder is equipped and more Essence was spent on warping to a Dreamgate than getting randomly from Enemies: 2.5% (1/40)
Essence rewards from the Seer 
100 Essence - Hallownest Seal
200 Essence - Spirits' Glade opens
300 Essence - Pale Ore
500 Essence - Dream Wielder Charm
700 Essence - Vessel Fragment
900 Essence -  Dreamgate
1200 Essence - Arcane Egg
1500 Essence - Mask Shard
1800 Essence - Awaken the Dream Nail and unlock the <i>Awakening</i> Achievement
2400 Essence - The <i>Ascension</i> Achievement
Achievements
Trivia 
The Dream Nail can be used to push back most enemies.
The amount of Essence that can be stored is capped by the 32-bit signed integer limit, which is 2,147,483,647 (over 2 billion).
Even though the Fluke Larvae near Flukemarm and in the  Junk Pit are not considered actual enemies in-game, they still have a chance to give 1 Essence after being defeated.
Certain NPCs can sense their mind being read, namely the White Lady, Snail Shaman, Bardoon, Seer and Midwife.
The backboard for Dream Nail dialogue is different for the Pale King's dialogue shown during the Birthplace memory. While all other Dream Nail dialogue uses a backboard with pink Essence, the backboard for dialogue during this scene has white Essence.
The <b>Dream Nail</b> is an Ability in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It can collect Essence and enter dreams.

# 文档 [288] Howling Wraiths
- 类别：skills
- 标识：howling-wraiths
- 路径：skills/howling-wraiths.json

# 技能/法术：Howling Wraiths
类型：spell
Casts three spectral wraiths above the Knight in a vertical arc. Best used against high-flying or grounded targets standing close enough.
效果：Unleash a cone of howling wraiths upward.
获取方式：Found in a sealed room within Howling Cliffs, accessed via the Mothwing Cloak.
所在区域：{'slug': 'howling-cliffs', 'name': 'Howling Cliffs'}
<b>Howling Wraiths</b> is a Spell in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. Using it releases a blast of SOUL above and around the Knight.
Function
Press FOCUS/CAST or QUICK CAST while holding UP to release a wave of energy in an arc around and above the Knight, dealing 3 hits.
At 6 times the strength of an Old Nail, it deals twice as much damage as Vengeful Spirit if all three hits connect.
The Spell has a wide range allowing for some hits even when the target is at an upper corner in relation to the Knight.
Like Vengeful Spirit, this Spell can stall the Knight in mid-air, though it does not send them in a direction opposite of the force.
Modifiers
Shaman Stone increases the damage dealt by Howling Wraiths by 50%.
Spell Twister lowers the SOUL cost to cast Howling Wraiths to 24 SOUL.
Can be upgraded to Abyss Shriek.
Damage Values
Charm
Damage Per Hit
Total Damage
None
13
39
Shaman Stone
20
60
How to Acquire
Found in the Overgrown Mound within Fog Canyon, next to the entrance to the Queen's Gardens.
Trivia
This Spell is found near the corpse of a snail shaman. Using the Dream Nail on this corpse yields the line:
<i>"...Hear...me..."</i>
After obtaining Howling Wraiths, the Knight's SOUL is completely refilled.
A Squit also spawns, just west of the Knight.
ZH:嚎叫幽灵

# 文档 [289] Isma's Tear
- 类别：skills
- 标识：ismas-tear
- 路径：skills/ismas-tear.json

# 技能/法术：Isma's Tear
类型：movement
Grants immunity to the acid that fills Royal Waterways and parts of Greenpath. Required for several mid-to-late-game routes.
效果：Walk and swim safely through pools of acid.
获取方式：Found in Isma's Grove, deep in the Royal Waterways.
所在区域：{'slug': 'ismas-grove', 'name': "Isma's Grove"}
<b>Isma's Tear</b> is an Ability in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It allows the Knight to swim in acid without taking damage.
Function
Although very useful, Isma's Tear is not necessary to complete the game. Obtaining it allows access to the following:
Shape of Unn in Greenpath
Access to Fog Canyon through Forgotten Crossroads or Fungal Wastes
A Grub in Isma's Grove
Access to the Queen's Gardens
A Grub as well as a shortcut in Kingdom's Edge
It is also useful while exploring Fog Canyon and fighting Uumuu.
How to Acquire
Located in Isma's Grove in the Royal Waterways. Accessing this area requires Crystal Heart and beating Dung Defender. A separate,much harder way to access it is by dashing, pogo-bouncing on the spikes then immediately dashing again. This method is almost impossible without frame-perfect timing.
Trivia
Dung Defender refers to it as "Isma's Blessing".
References
## CHARMS
共 10 篇文档
<b>Isma's Tear</b> is an Ability in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It allows the Knight to swim in acid without taking damage.
Function
Although very useful, Isma's Tear is not necessary to complete the game. Obtaining it allows access to the following:
Shape of Unn in Greenpath
Access to Fog Canyon through Forgotten Crossroads or Fungal Wastes
A Grub in Isma's Grove
Access to the Queen's Gardens
A Grub as well as a shortcut in Kingdom's Edge
It is also useful while exploring Fog Canyon and fighting Uumuu.
How to Acquire
Located in Isma's Grove in the Royal Waterways. Accessing this area requires Crystal Heart and beating Dung Defender. A separate,much harder way to access it is by dashing, pogo-bouncing on the spikes then immediately dashing again. This method is almost impossible without frame-perfect timing.
Trivia
Dung Defender refers to it as "Isma's Blessing".
References

# 文档 [290] Mantis Claw
- 类别：skills
- 标识：mantis-claw
- 路径：skills/mantis-claw.json

# 技能/法术：Mantis Claw
类型：movement
Allows the Knight to grip walls and leap off them. The single biggest exploration unlock in the entire game.
效果：Wall-cling and wall-jump from any vertical surface.
获取方式：Defeat the Mantis Lords in the Fungal Wastes.
所在区域：{'slug': 'mantis-village', 'name': 'Mantis Village'}
The <b>Mantis Claw</b> is an Ability in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It allows for clinging to walls and jumping off them.
Function
While close to a wall while in midair, press in the direction of the wall to cling to it and slide down. Press JUMP to launch diagonally away from the wall. This can be repeated an infinite number of times, allowing the Knight to climb up walls. Can only be used on completely vertical surfaces.
If both the RIGHT and LEFT buttons are pressed while sliding down a wall, the Knight slides at normal falling speed.
How to Acquire
Located in Mantis Village. Mothwing Cloak recommended.
The <b>Mantis Claw</b> is an Ability in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It allows for clinging to walls and jumping off them.
Function
While close to a wall while in midair, press in the direction of the wall to cling to it and slide down. Press JUMP to launch diagonally away from the wall. This can be repeated an infinite number of times, allowing the Knight to climb up walls. Can only be used on completely vertical surfaces.
If both the RIGHT and LEFT buttons are pressed while sliding down a wall, the Knight slides at normal falling speed.
How to Acquire
Located in Mantis Village. Mothwing Cloak recommended.

# 文档 [291] Monarch Wings
- 类别：skills
- 标识：monarch-wings
- 路径：skills/monarch-wings.json

# 技能/法术：Monarch Wings
类型：movement
Adds a double-jump that can be combined with the dash to reach almost anywhere. Required for the late-game traversal puzzles.
效果：Beat ethereal wings to double-jump in midair.
获取方式：Found in the Ancient Basin, in a chamber guarded by the Broken Vessel.
所在区域：{'slug': 'ancient-basin', 'name': 'Ancient Basin'}
The <b>Monarch Wings</b> are an Ability in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. It allows jumping again while in mid-air.
Function
Press JUMP while in the air to perform a double-jump. Refreshes when the Knight lands on the ground, bounces off an enemy/object with their Nail, or clings to/jumps off a wall using the Mantis Claw.
Similar to the regular jump the height of the "flap" scales with how long the JUMP button is held.
The Monarch Wings are not necessary to finish the game; however, they allow access to the following areas:
The Palace Grounds and consequently the White Palace.
The Fungal Core and consequently a Mask Shard.
The Enraged Guardian's room and consequently a Mask Shard.
The Monarch Wings are intended to be used to access Hallownest's Crown, the Watcher's Spire, the Hive, and Hornet in Kingdom's Edge. However, these locations can be accessed by Nail-bouncing on enemies and environmental objects.
The Monarch Wings are also very useful for platforming and during fights against some bosses.
The first frame of animation when using Monarch Wings does not immediately lift the Knight up, this is why there can be cases where the Knight gets hit by hazards below when falling despite the wings successfully manifesting.
How to Acquire
Located in the Ancient Basin, just after the Broken Vessel boss fight. The Crystal Heart is technically not required to reach this location.
Trivia
Collecting the Monarch Wings is one of the two triggers that causes the Forgotten Crossroads to become the Infected Crossroads (the other trigger being killing any of the Dreamers).
The official game manual describes the Monarch Wings as:
<i>"Wings of a monarchfly that grant momentary flight."</i>
The Monarch Wings are likely what cause the torrents of wind in portions of the Ancient Basin, as picking the Ability up stops the wind.
The Monarch Wings were originally called "Mantis Wings" on the Kickstarter page.
References

# 文档 [295] Vengeful Spirit
- 类别：skills
- 标识：vengeful-spirit
- 路径：skills/vengeful-spirit.json

# 技能/法术：Vengeful Spirit
类型：spell
Releases a horizontal spectral projectile. The Knight's first dedicated ranged attack and the path to Soul Master.
效果：Launch a vengeful spirit at enemies.
获取方式：Taught by the Snail Shaman in the Ancestral Mound.
所在区域：{'slug': 'ancestral-mound', 'name': 'Ancestral Mound'}
<b>Vengeful Spirit</b> is a Spell in <i>Hollow Knight</i>. Using it conjures a spirit that flies forward and damages enemies.
Function
Press FOCUS/CAST or QUICK CAST without holding UP or DOWN to launch a projectile that passes through enemies and deals damage. The projectile passes through invulnerable parts of an enemy, such as a shield or shell, but will not damage a fully protected enemy.
Before any other Spells have been acquired, Vengeful Spirit is cast regardless of the direction being held.
Modifiers
The Flukenest Charm turns Vengeful Spirit into a horde of baby flukes that bounce around dealing damage. This is particularly powerful up close, and damage falls off with distance.
When combined with the Defender's Crest Charm, launches a single large fluke that explodes into a damage-dealing cloud of gas.
The Shaman Stone Charm increases the size of the projectile and the damage dealt by 33%.
The Spell Twister Charm lowers the SOUL cost to cast Vengeful Spirit to 24 SOUL.
Can be upgraded into Shade Soul.
Damage Values
Charm
colspan=3|Damage
None
colspan=3|15
Shaman Stone
colspan=3|20
Charm
colspan=2|Damage Per Hit
Total Damage
Flukenest
colspan=2|4

Flukenest + Shaman Stone

Flukenest + Defender's Crest + Shaman Stone
3
1
32
How to Acquire
It is given by the Snail Shaman located in the Ancestral Mound in the Forgotten Crossroads.
Trivia
A cut inventory description for Vengeful Spirit can be found in the game's files:
<i>"A desire for revenge is seared into the SOUL of those who fell in battle or were wronged in life. A Shaman can concentrate this desire and cast it out into the world to burn away whatever stands before them."</i>
With the Vengeful Spirit Spell, the Elder Baldur blocking the way to Greenpath can be killed. This is the intended way to access the rest of the areas in the game.
It is possible to reach the Resting Grounds and obtain the Dream Nail before Vengeful Spirit by buying the Lumafly Lantern from Sly and entering Crystal Peak with it.
It is also possible to defeat the Elder Baldur in other ways, though they are extremely difficult. For example, by using the  Dreamshield or Longnail Charm.
Vengeful Spirit pushes the Knight backwards slightly. This allows crossing some gaps that would otherwise be impassable without assistance; for example, in Greenpath, it is possible to skip to the ledge where Hornet is first encountered.
After obtaining Vengeful Spirit, the Knight's SOUL is completely refilled when they wake up.
Notes

# 文档 [296] Colosseum of Fools
- 类别：quests
- 标识：colosseum_of_fools
- 路径：wiki/Colosseum_of_Fools

# 任务：Colosseum of Fools
The **Colosseum of Fools** is an area located at the top of Kingdom's Edge. It contains an arena where the Knight may participate in three Trials in which they battle waves of enemies.
Description
The Colosseum of Fools is located in the carved-out shell of a massive, ancient bug. Many chains can be seen which hold this shell in place. Trials can be selected inside the head of the shell, where Little Fool oversees payment. The fights themselves take place in the arena east of the trial boards.
Below the arena is a warriors' pit with a Bench and several non-hostile Fools. Tiso can be found on the Bench if he was listened to at all previous points. Zote is located here too if he was saved in Deepnest. To the west of the warriors' pit is a room where the Knight's Shade spawns if the Knight was killed during a Trial. At the very east end of the warriors' pit is a Hot Spring with a Sturdy Fool relaxing in it.
The east side of the arena can be seen from the warriors' pit. Sounds of battle and cheering from the crowd can be heard, thrown weapons of Sturdy Fools and squishes of the Infection can be seen on the other side of the gate, though no enemies are visible and the gate cannot be opened or broken. A breakable wall to the very east of this leads to an area outside the back of the Colosseum. The  Pale Lurker is found here where she can be killed for a Simple Key.
Lore
The strongest warriors from all corners are drawn to Hallownest to compete in the Colosseum, where only the strongest survive. Contestants are offered the chance to become more than just another foolish bug, as they aim to take the title of champion of the Colosseum. Lord Fool oversaw the fights in the arena, and some bugs were determined to prove their strength to them. The corpses of those who die in the arena are cast into the chasm below the Colosseum.
When the Crystal Heart is Charged on a temporary wall in the Trials, the knight remains in place even after the wall retracts (usually because companions defeated the current enemy), showing the crystals and the knight suspended in midair unless otherwise disturbed.
In the entrance to the pale lurker's area, you can watch a tiny bit of the fight happening in the colosseum. No characters appear, but infection particles and sturdy fool projectiles can be seen.
The sturdy fool projectiles can be deflected to interfere with the fight.
*"Colosseum squeaked in there late in development. We were talking about potentially releasing it as a free DLC (this is before we had the idea of content packs) but after discussion we decided that having a place to really test your combat skills was important to have. Also, removing it would have left a weird empty gap at the top of Kingdom's Edge!"* - William Pellen
*"The Colosseum does hide a secret, and there's a chance we'll explore it in the future. I'm trying to remember how many extra bosses we did put in the colosseum. Zote was one. Those Fat bees were another... Two of the Colosseum warriors were originally bosses, but we liked them so much we transformed them into regular foes. It's all a bit of a blur!"* -Ari Gibson
The Colosseum of Fools was originally meant to be in Fungal Wastes.
---

# 文档 [297] Delicate Flower
- 类别：quests
- 标识：delicate_flower
- 路径：merged

# 任务：Delicate Flower
## Overview

The **Delicate Flower** is an Item in *Hollow Knight*. It can be given to various NPCs. The flower is very fragile and will be destroyed if you take damage or ride the Stagways.

## Lore

The flowers originate from outside of Hallownest from a place known as "lands serene". They were brought to the kingdom by the great knight Ze'mer, who is now the Grey Mourner. They glow faintly with pale light. There is a rare power hidden in their fragile petals. Godseeker wonders if the flowers are splinters of something greater, but is unable to figure out whether this is true, as she cannot detect a resonance from it.

## Starting Location

The quest is initiated by speaking to the Grey Mourner, located in the Resting Grounds near the entrance to the Grey Mansion. Being near the entrance to the Grey Mansion automatically sets the Knight's save point to the Bench just outside.

## Objectives

The primary objective is to deliver the Delicate Flower to the grave of the Traitors' Child in the Queen's Gardens without destroying it. The flower will be destroyed if you:
- Take any damage
- Ride the Stagways
- Use the Dreamgate

Note: Riding the Trams or Elevators will NOT destroy the Delicate Flower.

If the flower is destroyed or given to an NPC, the quest can be attempted again by accepting another flower from the Grey Mourner.

After the quest is completed and the Grey Mourner has departed, additional flowers can be acquired. These can be found growing near the grave where the original flower was delivered. The Delicate Flower taken from the grave comes with a different description:
*"Taken from the Queen's Gardens. It glows faintly with pale light."*
*"The flower is very fragile and will be destroyed if you take damage or ride the Stagways."*

Taking the flower from the Queen's Gardens does not automatically set the Bench. This can be used to teleport to any Bench with the flower, making it much easier to deliver it to a location. This can be done by sitting on a Bench, travelling to the Queen's Gardens and picking up the flower, and then quitting to the menu. Flowers picked up from the Queen's Gardens do not appear in the inventory when destroyed.

## Rewards

Successfully completing this quest by taking the undamaged flower to the Traitors' Child's grave and then returning to Grey Mourner rewards a **Mask Shard**.

When the flower is given to Godseeker in the Junk Pit, a new ending is unlocked.

## Possible Recipients

- **Grave of the Traitors' Child** (primary quest target)
- **Elderbug**
- **Nailmaster Oro** (Regardless of pantheon encounter)
- **The Godseeker** (After completing two Pantheons)

Additionally, it is possible to offer a flower to **Eternal Emilitia** and the **White Lady**, though they both decline the offer.

## Achievements

*(No specific achievement names were listed in the source data, but the quest completion and alternate endings are tied to in-game achievements.)*

## Trivia

- Blocking a hit with the **Baldur Shell** Charm equipped does not destroy the Delicate Flower, but avoiding damage with **Carefree Melody** does.
- Taking damage with the flower in the inventory lets out a burst of petals in a unique hit animation.
- While riding the Stagways breaks the flower, riding the Trams does not.
---

# 文档 [298] Grimm Troupe
- 类别：quests
- 标识：grimm_troupe
- 路径：merged

# 任务：Grimm Troupe
## Overview

**The Grimm Troupe** is the second of the three free content packs planned for *Hollow Knight*. Its name and content were revealed on September 14th, 2017. It was released on October 26th, 2017. This update added a major quest with its own characters and bosses, several Charms, and a platforming challenge.

## Starting Location

The quest begins by interacting with a **Grimmsteed** (a large, sleeping bug) found in **Howling Cliffs**. After striking the Grimmsteed with the Dream Nail, the **Grimm Troupe** is summoned to Dirtmouth, where a new tent appears.

## Objectives

The main quest involves aiding the Grimm Troupe in their ritual. Key objectives include:

- **Lighting the Nightmare Lantern**: The player must collect **Flames** from three **Grimmkin** enemies (Grimmkin Novice, Grimmkin Master, Grimmkin Nightmare) located in various areas of Hallownest.
- **Defeating Grimm**: After collecting all flames, the player can challenge **Grimm** inside the tent. Defeating Grimm grants an **Additional Charm Notch**.
- **The Nightmare's Heart**: After defeating Grimm, the player can choose to either:
  - **Banish the Troupe**: Speak to **Brumm** (the musician) in the tent, then defeat the **Nightmare King** (a harder version of Grimm) to banish the Troupe. This rewards the **Carefree Melody** charm.
  - **Complete the Ritual**: Defeat the **Nightmare King** directly. This rewards the **Grimmchild** charm upgrade.
- **Path of Pain**: A hidden, extremely difficult platforming challenge located in the **White Palace**. Completing it rewards the **Seal of Binding** and unlocks a new **Menu Theme**.
- **Nymm**: After banishing the Troupe, **Brumm** becomes **Nymm** and appears in Dirtmouth, selling the **Unbreakable Strength**, **Unbreakable Heart**, and **Unbreakable Greed** charms (previously upgraded by **Divine**).

## Rewards

- **Charms**:
  - **Grimmchild** (upgraded from the base charm)
  - **Dreamshield** (upgraded)
  - **Sprintmaster**
  - **Weaversong**
  - **Carefree Melody** (obtained by banishing the Troupe)
  - **Unbreakable Strength**
  - **Unbreakable Heart**
  - **Unbreakable Greed**
- **Additional Charm Notch** (gained by defeating Grimm)
- **Seal of Binding** (from Path of Pain)
- **The Grimm Troupe menu style** (unlocked after completing Path of Pain)
- **3 new achievements**
- **Menu Theme** (new music for the main menu)

## Lore

The Grimm Troupe is a mysterious traveling circus that performs a dark ritual. They are led by **Grimm**, the master of the Troupe, and serve the **Nightmare's Heart**, a powerful entity that feeds on the dreams of Hallownest. The Troupe includes:
- **Grimm** (boss)
- **Nightmare King** (secret boss)
- **Grimmkin Novice**, **Grimmkin Master**, **Grimmkin Nightmare** (flame-collecting enemies)
- **Grimmchild** (companion charm)
- **Brumm** (musician, later becomes **Nymm**)
- **Divine** (charm upgrade vendor)
- **Grimmsteed** (the sleeping bug that triggers the quest)

The ritual involves collecting **Flames** from across Hallownest to fuel the Nightmare's Heart. The player can either complete the ritual (defeating the Nightmare King) or banish the Troupe (with Brumm's help), each leading to different outcomes and rewards.
---

# 文档 [299] Hunter's Journal
- 类别：quests
- 标识：hunters_journal
- 路径：merged

# 任务：Hunter's Journal
## Overview

The **Hunter's Journal** is a compendium of every enemy found in *Hellow Knight*. Most new entries are added to the Journal after defeating new enemies. Defeating a specified number of each enemy unlocks additional notes from the Hunter about that enemy, as well as bits of lore, techniques for fighting said enemy, or even information about the Hunter himself. A few entries can only be obtained by inspecting a specific object or as a reward for completing a challenge. After completing most entries, the Hunter's Mark can be acquired. DLC enemies do not count.

A total of 168 entries can be acquired for the Hunter's Journal. However, four of these entries — the Hunter's Mark, Seal of Binding, Void Idol, and Weathered Mask — do not increase the total entry count. This means the Journal only counts 164 entries. There are 146 entries required for the *Keen Hunter* Achievement. In order to see the number of creatures encountered and the total number required to complete the journal, the World Sense ability must be acquired.

Completed entries in the Hunter's Journal have a different border around their icons.

## Starting Location

The Hunter's Journal is dropped on the ground by the Hunter in Greenpath after listening to him for the first time. When it is inspected, the Journal can be found as a pane in the Menu.

## Objectives

The objective is to fill the Hunter's Journal by defeating enemies and adding their details. Most entries are added after defeating new enemies. A few entries can only be obtained by inspecting a specific object or as a reward for completing a challenge. Defeating a specified number of each enemy unlocks additional notes from the Hunter.

## Rewards

After completing most entries, the Hunter's Mark can be acquired. DLC enemies do not count toward this reward.

## Lore

The Hunter's Journal was first revealed in a Kickstarter update:

*"What's everyone's favourite part of any game? That's right - filling out a bestiary by killing bad guys! Then reading about them! At least, it's one of our favourite bits, so we couldn't resist adding the feature to Hollow Knight. If you explore the Greenpath carefully, you'll come across the mysterious Hunter in his lair. He'll give you his Hunter's Journal, and charge you with the task of defeating enemies, adding their details to the journal. And so your hunt begins! Defeating enemies will now add entries to the journal which you can check out whenever you have a quiet moment. As you defeat more of a certain enemy, you'll start to decipher the Hunter's notes and gain some insight into the creatures of Hallownest as well as the Hunter himself. We've had a lot of fun building the Hunter's Journal, and we hope you'll enjoy seeking out rare beasts and filling out entries. If you manage to complete the journal entirely, head back to see the Hunter so you can receive your well-deserved reward..."*

# 文档 [300] Crystal Heart
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：crystal_heart
- 路径：wiki/Crystal_Heart

# 能力：Crystal Heart
**Crystal Heart** is an Ability in *Hollow Knight*. It allows the Knight to fly forward horizontally until colliding with a wall or enemy that is not killed by the dash.
Function
Hold SUPER DASH while on the ground or clinging to a wall to concentrate force. Release the button at full charge to blast forwards and fly through the air. The Knight continues moving forward until interrupted by damage or the environment, by pressing JUMP or by tapping SUPER DASH again.
The Super Dash deals 10 damage on contact with an enemy, and any enemy killed by this hit does not damage the Knight or stop their movement.
How to Acquire
Found in an old mining golem at the end of a platforming segment in Crystal Peak. Requires Mantis Claw.
Trivia
It takes 0.8 seconds to charge the Crystal Heart.
It is possible to use the Dream Nail on the old mining golem, which gives the following dialogue:
"DIG...DIG...CRUSH...DIG...LIFT...DIG...LIFT...DIG...
CRUSH...OBEY...DIG...LIFT...CRUSH...DROP...
DROP...DIG...LIFT...DIG...CRUSH...OBEY...DIG...
DIG...DIG...LIFT...FOLLOW...OBEY...FOLLOW...OBEY...
CRUSH...CRUSH...OBEY...CRUSH...OBEY...CRUSH...
CRUSH...CRUSH...CRUSH...CRUSH...CRUSH...CRUSH..."
---

# 文档 [301] Desolate Dive
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：desolate_dive
- 路径：wiki/Desolate_Dive

# 能力：Desolate Dive
**Desolate Dive** is a Spell in *Hollow Knight*. Using it strikes the ground with concentrated SOUL, breaking floors and damaging enemies.
Function
Press FOCUS/CAST or QUICK CAST while holding DOWN to cause the Knight to slam into the ground, creating a shockwave that spreads out and up. The dive deals 15 damage, while the shockwave deals 20.
The Knight is invincible for 0.4 seconds during and after using Desolate Dive. This allows for chaining uses of Desolate Dive to avoid enemy damage as long as the Knight has enough SOUL. Using Desolate Dive in quick succession cancels the invincibility frames of the Spell if it is cast while the previous Spell's invincibility frames have not yet run out.
Desolate Dive also allows breaking certain floors, such as those to exit the Soul Sanctum and to enter Crystal Peak.
Modifiers
Shaman Stone increases the damage dealt by Desolate Dive by 51%.
Spell Twister lowers the SOUL cost to cast Desolate Dive to 24 SOUL.
Can be upgraded to Descending Dark.
Damage Values
Charm
Dive Damage
Shockwave Damage
Total Damage
None
15
20
35
Shaman Stone
23
30
53
How to Acquire
Reward for defeating Soul Master in the City of Tears.
Trivia
Desolate Dive was revealed in a Kickstarter update where it was referred to as the **Tyrant's Fist**:
*"This ancient, royal magic allows you to focus energy into your fist and slam it down into the ground, releasing a shockwave that blows away foes and can even rupture the earth you stand on!"*
Descending Dark and Desolate Dive can be used while Dung Defender is underground to force him out and stagger him.
After obtaining Desolate Dive, the Knight's SOUL is completely refilled.
References

# 文档 [302] Dream Nail
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：dream_nail
- 路径：wiki/Dream_Nail

# 能力：Dream Nail
The **Dream Nail** is an Ability in *Hollow Knight*. It can collect Essence and enter dreams.
Lore
The Dream Nail is a sacred weapon and talisman, which can cut the veil that separates the waking world from dreams. It appears to have been made by the Moth Tribe. The Dream Nail allows its user to not only read the thoughts of an entity, or even inanimate objects, but also enter specific sections of the Dream Realm.
Before the Knight acquires it, the blade dulled over time, making it necessary to fill it with enough Essence to awaken it. Essence are the fragments of light that dreams are composed of. Dreams can also take the shape of those who have passed away. Dreams and memories cling onto the Dream Nail when Essence is collected.
Another one of the Dream Nail's abilities is to teleport the user from one place to another through dreams. The user warps by imagining a great gate to a location connected to them, provided the location has a strong connection to dreams.
Function
Hold down DREAM NAIL to charge and swing the Dream Nail. This can perform several functions:
Extract Essence from Spirits
Activate Whispering Roots
Collect SOUL from living enemies (33 SOUL)
Challenge Warrior Dreams
Read the minds of NPCs, Enemies (excluding Warrior Dreams), and some statues and corpses
Instantly kill both the Shade and Siblings
Summon  The Grimm Troupe
Use to set or travel to a  Dreamgate (Requires 900 Essence)
Enter the Dream Realm
Challenge Dream Bosses
Access the Shrine of Believers
Enter the minds of Dreamers
Access the White Palace (Awoken Dream Nail, requires 1800 Essence)
Access  Godhome
Obtain Void Heart
Challenge the Radiance
Switch boss forms in the  Hall of Gods
The Dream Wielder Charm, granted by the Seer after collecting 500 Essence, greatly reduces the charge time of the Dream Nail and doubles the SOUL gained from hitting living enemies (from 33 to 66).
How to Acquire
The Dream Nail is acquired in the Resting Grounds by inspecting the Dreamers Memorial. Doing so sends the Knight into a dream where they receive the Dream Nail from a Moth.
 Awoken Dream Nail
After collecting 1800 Essence, the Dream Nail can be awoken. This allows access to dreams and memories that were previously hidden. The Awoken Dream Nail can be used on the corpse of the Kingsmould in the Palace Grounds. This grants entry to the White Palace.
Furthermore, the Awoken Dream Nail can be used to view the Dream Nail dialogue of the Shade Cloak creature in the Abyss. This creature has different Dream Nail dialogue depending on whether Void Heart has been obtained.
Essence
Essence is the energy gained from multiple sources after obtaining the Dream Nail. After obtaining certain amounts of Essence, the Knight can return to the Seer for rewards. A total of 2400 is needed for all in-game rewards and achievements, though up to 3208 essence is available from exploration and bosses. Warping using the Dreamgate uses 1 Essence each time.
Essence Sources
Using Dream Nail on a Spirit (26 total)
Collecting Essence spawned by a Whispering Root (482 total)
Defeating a Warrior Dream (1100 total)
Elder Hu (100)
Galien (200)
Gorb (100)
Markoth (250)
Marmu (150)
No Eyes (200)
Xero (100)
Defeating a Dream Boss (1600 total)
Failed Champion (300)
Grey Prince Zote (300)
Lost Kin (400)
White Defender (300)
Soul Tyrant (300)
Regular enemies have a chance to drop Essence:
If less Essence was spent on warping to a Dreamgate than getting randomly from Enemies: 0.33% (1/300)
If more Essence was spent on warping to a Dreamgate than getting randomly from Enemies: 1.67% (1/60)
If Dream Wielder is equipped and less Essence was spent on warping to a Dreamgate than getting randomly from Enemies: 0.5% (1/200)
If Dream Wielder is equipped and more Essence was spent on warping to a Dreamgate than getting randomly from Enemies: 2.5% (1/40)
Essence rewards from the Seer 
100 Essence - Hallownest Seal
200 Essence - Spirits' Glade opens
300 Essence - Pale Ore
500 Essence - Dream Wielder Charm
700 Essence - Vessel Fragment
900 Essence -  Dreamgate
1200 Essence - Arcane Egg
1500 Essence - Mask Shard
1800 Essence - Awaken the Dream Nail and unlock the *Awakening* Achievement
2400 Essence - The *Ascension* Achievement
Achievements
Trivia 
The Dream Nail can be used to push back most enemies.
The amount of Essence that can be stored is capped by the 32-bit signed integer limit, which is 2,147,483,647 (over 2 billion).
Even though the Fluke Larvae near Flukemarm and in the  Junk Pit are not considered actual enemies in-game, they still have a chance to give 1 Essence after being defeated.
Certain NPCs can sense their mind being read, namely the White Lady, Snail Shaman, Bardoon, Seer and Midwife.
The backboard for Dream Nail dialogue is different for the Pale King's dialogue shown during the Birthplace memory. While all other Dream Nail dialogue uses a backboard with pink Essence, the backboard for dialogue during this scene has white Essence.
---

# 文档 [303] Howling Wraiths
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：howling_wraiths
- 路径：wiki/Howling_Wraiths

# 能力：Howling Wraiths
**Howling Wraiths** is a Spell in *Hollow Knight*. Using it releases a blast of SOUL above and around the Knight.
Function
Press FOCUS/CAST or QUICK CAST while holding UP to release a wave of energy in an arc around and above the Knight, dealing 3 hits.
At 6 times the strength of an Old Nail, it deals twice as much damage as Vengeful Spirit if all three hits connect.
The Spell has a wide range allowing for some hits even when the target is at an upper corner in relation to the Knight.
Like Vengeful Spirit, this Spell can stall the Knight in mid-air, though it does not send them in a direction opposite of the force.
Modifiers
Shaman Stone increases the damage dealt by Howling Wraiths by 50%.
Spell Twister lowers the SOUL cost to cast Howling Wraiths to 24 SOUL.
Can be upgraded to Abyss Shriek.
Damage Values

How to Acquire
Found in the Overgrown Mound within Fog Canyon, next to the entrance to the Queen's Gardens.
Trivia
This Spell is found near the corpse of a snail shaman. Using the Dream Nail on this corpse yields the line:
*"...Hear...me..."*
After obtaining Howling Wraiths, the Knight's SOUL is completely refilled.
A Squit also spawns, just west of the Knight.

# 文档 [304] Isma's Tear
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：ismas_tear
- 路径：wiki/Isma's_Tear

# 能力：Isma's Tear
**Isma's Tear** is an Ability in *Hollow Knight*. It allows the Knight to swim in acid without taking damage.
Function
Although very useful, Isma's Tear is not necessary to complete the game. Obtaining it allows access to the following:
Shape of Unn in Greenpath
Access to Fog Canyon through Forgotten Crossroads or Fungal Wastes
A Grub in Isma's Grove
Access to the Queen's Gardens
A Grub as well as a shortcut in Kingdom's Edge
It is also useful while exploring Fog Canyon and fighting Uumuu.
How to Acquire
Located in Isma's Grove in the Royal Waterways. Accessing this area requires Crystal Heart and beating Dung Defender. A separate,much harder way to access it is by dashing, pogo-bouncing on the spikes then immediately dashing again. This method is almost impossible without frame-perfect timing.
Trivia
Dung Defender refers to it as "Isma's Blessing".
References
---

# 文档 [305] King's Brand
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：kings_brand
- 路径：merged

# 能力：King's Brand
## Overview

The **King's Brand** is an Item in *Hollow Knight*. It marks anyone who bears it as the King of Hallownest.

## Function

Allows access to the door at the bottom of the Ancient Basin leading to the Abyss, which is required to unlock four endings. Also adds new dialogue for Bardoon, Eternal Emilitia, Mask Maker, Steel Soul Jinn, Midwife, and the White Lady.

## How to Obtain

The King's Brand is located in the Cast-Off Shell in Kingdom's Edge, guarded by Hornet. After Hornet is defeated, the King's Brand can be acquired at the very end of the Cast-Off Shell.

Normally requires Monarch Wings to access, but can be accessed early by Nail-bouncing on a Primal Aspid.

## Trivia

After the Knight is marked with the King's Brand, the Cast-Off Shell starts falling apart. Hornet saves the Knight from being buried under the shell's pieces.
---

# 文档 [306] Mantis Claw
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：mantis_claw
- 路径：wiki/Mantis_Claw

# 能力：Mantis Claw
The **Mantis Claw** is an Ability in *Hollow Knight*. It allows for clinging to walls and jumping off them.
Function
While close to a wall while in midair, press in the direction of the wall to cling to it and slide down. Press JUMP to launch diagonally away from the wall. This can be repeated an infinite number of times, allowing the Knight to climb up walls. Can only be used on completely vertical surfaces.
If both the RIGHT and LEFT buttons are pressed while sliding down a wall, the Knight slides at normal falling speed.
How to Acquire
Located in Mantis Village. Mothwing Cloak recommended.
---

# 文档 [307] Monarch Wings
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：monarch_wings
- 路径：wiki/Monarch_Wings

# 能力：Monarch Wings
The **Monarch Wings** are an Ability in *Hollow Knight*. It allows jumping again while in mid-air.
Function
Press JUMP while in the air to perform a double-jump. Refreshes when the Knight lands on the ground, bounces off an enemy/object with their Nail, or clings to/jumps off a wall using the Mantis Claw.
Similar to the regular jump the height of the "flap" scales with how long the JUMP button is held.
The Monarch Wings are not necessary to finish the game; however, they allow access to the following areas:
The Palace Grounds and consequently the White Palace.
The Fungal Core and consequently a Mask Shard.
The Enraged Guardian's room and consequently a Mask Shard.
The Monarch Wings are intended to be used to access Hallownest's Crown, the Watcher's Spire, the Hive, and Hornet in Kingdom's Edge. However, these locations can be accessed by Nail-bouncing on enemies and environmental objects.
The Monarch Wings are also very useful for platforming and during fights against some bosses.
The first frame of animation when using Monarch Wings does not immediately lift the Knight up, this is why there can be cases where the Knight gets hit by hazards below when falling despite the wings successfully manifesting.
How to Acquire
Located in the Ancient Basin, just after the Broken Vessel boss fight. The Crystal Heart is technically not required to reach this location.
Trivia
Collecting the Monarch Wings is one of the two triggers that causes the Forgotten Crossroads to become the Infected Crossroads (the other trigger being killing any of the Dreamers).
The official game manual describes the Monarch Wings as:
*"Wings of a monarchfly that grant momentary flight."*
The Monarch Wings are likely what cause the torrents of wind in portions of the Ancient Basin, as picking the Ability up stops the wind.
The Monarch Wings were originally called "Mantis Wings" on the Kickstarter page.
References
---

# 文档 [308] Nail
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：nail
- 路径：merged

# 能力：Nail
## Overview

**Nail** is the term used to describe the bladed weapons wielded by several enemies, NPCs, and bosses in *Hollow Knight*, including the Knight. The Knight's Nail is a traditional weapon of Hallownest, and its damage can be increased through upgrades and certain Charms.

The **Fragile Strength** / **Unbreakable Strength** and **Fury of the Fallen** Charms also increase Nail damage.

## How to Obtain

The Knight begins the game with the **Nail** as their default weapon. No purchase or discovery is required.

## Function

The Nail is the Knight's primary melee weapon. Its base damage can be increased by upgrading it at the **Nailsmith** in the **City of Tears**. The Nailsmith can upgrade the Knight's Nail up to 4 times using **Geo** and **Pale Ore**, which increase the damage of Nail strikes.

### Nail Upgrades

| Upgrade | Description | Cost | Damage |
|---------|-------------|------|--------|
| **Nail** (default) | *A traditional weapon of Hallownest. Its blade is blunt with age and wear.* | Default weapon | 5 |
| **Sharpened Nail** | *A traditional weapon of Hallownest, restored to lethal form.* | 250 Geo | 9 |
| **Channelled Nail** | *A cleft weapon of Hallownest. The blade is exquisitely balanced.* | 800 Geo + 1 Pale Ore | 13 |
| **Coiled Nail** | *A powerful weapon of Hallownest, refined beyond all others.* | 2000 Geo + 2 Pale Ore | 17 |
| **Pure Nail** | *The ultimate weapon of Hallownest. Crafted to perfection, this ancient nail reveals its true form.* | 4000 Geo + 3 Pale Ore | 21 |
---

# 文档 [309] Vengeful Spirit
- 类别：abilities
- 标识：vengeful_spirit
- 路径：wiki/Vengeful_Spirit

# 能力：Vengeful Spirit
**Vengeful Spirit** is a Spell in *Hollow Knight*. Using it conjures a spirit that flies forward and damages enemies.
Function
Press FOCUS/CAST or QUICK CAST without holding UP or DOWN to launch a projectile that passes through enemies and deals damage. The projectile passes through invulnerable parts of an enemy, such as a shield or shell, but will not damage a fully protected enemy.
Before any other Spells have been acquired, Vengeful Spirit is cast regardless of the direction being held.
Modifiers
The Flukenest Charm turns Vengeful Spirit into a horde of baby flukes that bounce around dealing damage. This is particularly powerful up close, and damage falls off with distance.
When combined with the Defender's Crest Charm, launches a single large fluke that explodes into a damage-dealing cloud of gas.
The Shaman Stone Charm increases the size of the projectile and the damage dealt by 33%.
The Spell Twister Charm lowers the SOUL cost to cast Vengeful Spirit to 24 SOUL.
Can be upgraded into Shade Soul.
Damage Values
Charm
colspan=3|Damage
None
colspan=3|15
Shaman Stone
colspan=3|20
Charm
colspan=2|Damage Per Hit
Total Damage
Flukenest
colspan=2|4
36
Flukenest + Shaman Stone
colspan=2|5

How to Acquire
It is given by the Snail Shaman located in the Ancestral Mound in the Forgotten Crossroads.
Trivia
A cut inventory description for Vengeful Spirit can be found in the game's files:
*"A desire for revenge is seared into the SOUL of those who fell in battle or were wronged in life. A Shaman can concentrate this desire and cast it out into the world to burn away whatever stands before them."*
With the Vengeful Spirit Spell, the Elder Baldur blocking the way to Greenpath can be killed. This is the intended way to access the rest of the areas in the game.
It is possible to reach the Resting Grounds and obtain the Dream Nail before Vengeful Spirit by buying the Lumafly Lantern from Sly and entering Crystal Peak with it.
It is also possible to defeat the Elder Baldur in other ways, though they are extremely difficult. For example, by using the  Dreamshield or Longnail Charm.
Vengeful Spirit pushes the Knight backwards slightly. This allows crossing some gaps that would otherwise be impassable without assistance; for example, in Greenpath, it is possible to skip to the ledge where Hornet is first encountered.
After obtaining Vengeful Spirit, the Knight's SOUL is completely refilled when they wake up.
Notes

# 文档 [310] Abyss Creature
- 类别：lore
- 标识：abyss_creature
- 路径：wiki/Abyss_Creature

# Lore：Abyss Creature
In the room containing the Lifeblood Core Charm, a massive, multi-eyed head can be seen opening its eyes in the foggy background, moving up and down slightly as if breathing. It makes no noise, and cannot be interacted with in any way. It is referred to in the game files as "Abyss Creature", though only the head sprite exists for it. Any specific relations to Lifeblood or the rest of the events in Hallownest are, as of yet, unknown.
The Abyss Creature can be seen again in a room behind the blue door in Godhome. The meaning behind this appearance is again currently unknown but furthers the connection between this being and Lifeblood.
---

# 文档 [311] Ancient Civilisation
- 类别：lore
- 标识：ancient_civilisation
- 路径：wiki/Ancient_Civilisation

# Lore：Ancient Civilisation
The **ancient civilisation** was a civilisation of bugs that existed in the distant past before the Kingdom of Hallownest was founded. This civilisation did not devote its worship to any lord or power but instead worshipped the Void itself.
Soul Totems
Soul Totems are remnants of the ancient civilisation.
Several Soul Totems can be found in Deepnest in the Sharp Shadow area. These Soul Totems have Void tendrils attached to them which appears to have corrupted them, forming the Sharp Shadow Charm. This Charm contains a forbidden Spell that transforms shadows into deadly weapons and bears a resemblance to the shape of one of the Soul Totems.
Arcane Eggs
Relics created by the ancient civilisation, Arcane Eggs are stone eggs that contain knowledge hidden within. Most of these eggs are found in the Abyss. An egg is a perfect protective form. While the kingdom of Hallownest used stone journals or tablets to store information, the Arcane Eggs have their records stored within their multiple layers.
Extracting this knowledge is difficult and painstaking work for relic seekers such as Relic Seeker Lemm, making them only able to access the outer layer of the eggs in fear of damaging them.
 Void Idol
The Void Idol is a rare artifact belonging to the ancient civilisation. Its Journal entry is obtained after defeating all bosses in the Hall of Gods on Attuned difficulty. Defeating all bosses on Ascended and Radiant changes the state of the idol. The first state of the Void Idol contains only a drop of Void. The imperfect nails which were discarded in this attempt eventually fused together to form the Quick Slash Charm. It is not known if the ancient Nailsmith was successful in creating a Pure Nail. Its Dream Nail dialogue, *"Pure"*, is the same as that of the Nailsmith's corpse after he has forged the Knight's Pure Nail. The hallway leading up to this room also has architecture similar to the Temple of the Black Egg and those found near many Soul Totems.
Shade Beast
This bug holds the Void bowl in which the Shade Cloak is acquired. In the game's files, it is called "Shade Beast". When the unawoken Dream Nail is used on it, a possible seal appears over its head. Its Dream Nail dialogue can only be seen with the Awoken Dream Nail. Before obtaining Void Heart, this creature claims that the Void has power if it is unified. After the Knight has Void Heart, its dialogue changes, referring to them as the Lord of Shades.
Green Beast
The giant six-eyed corpse of this bug is seen in the Queen's Gardens. Its file name is "Green Beast". There is no other information on this bug besides its file name and appearance.
Colosseum of Fools corpse
The Colosseum of Fools is built inside the carved out shell of an ancient bug, located at the top of the ashen cliffs of Kingdom's Edge. It has six eyes, and two claws near the front of its body. From the way it appears on the Map for Kingdom's Edge, it seems that it has a segmented torso. Not much else is known about this bug other than its current purpose as a location for the Colosseum.
Temple of the Black Egg shell
The exterior of the Temple of the Black Egg was fashioned from the shell of an ancient bug. Its head has six horns, with several more horns located on its segmented lower body. The origin of the Black Egg inside the Temple is unknown.
Beast's Den shrine
A room located in the west part of Beast's Den contains an unknown being. The file names for the sprites in this room refer to the area as a "shrine". Hitting the being with the Nail produces a metallic sound. Hitting it with Spells makes a seal appear over it. It is unclear if this being is the corpse of an ancient bug or a statue.
Trivia
The Shade Beast, Green Beast, and the Beast's Den shrine are shown in various concept sketches.
---

# 文档 [312] Arcane Egg

# Items：Arcane Egg
**Arcane Eggs** are jet black stone eggs originating from a civilisation that existed before the Kingdom of Hallownest was founded. According to Relic Seeker Lemm, each of these eggs contains knowledge and records within its various layers, although only the outer layer is accessible to Lemm. Other Relic Seekers claim that there is a will within these eggs, with each seeking its own bearer, but Lemm remains sceptical of those claims.
Use
Can be sold to Relic Seeker Lemm for .
Shop description:
Ah! This seems like a simple egg, but it's actually a precious relic from before the birth of Hallownest!
I'll pay you a small fortune for it. Please sell it to me!
How to Acquire
There are a total of 4 Arcane Eggs that can be obtained:
3 found in the Abyss
1 located below the room in a secret path where Lifeblood Core is found
1 directly west of where Shade Cloak is acquired
1 in the south part of the Birthplace (requires Kingsoul)
1 given by the Seer in the Resting Grounds as a reward for 1,200 Essence
References

# 文档 [313] Armoured Squit
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：armoured_squit
- 路径：wiki/Armoured_Squit

# Enemies：Armoured Squit
**Armoured Squits** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are descendants of the Squit, bred exclusively for battle in the Colosseum of Fools.
Behaviour and Tactics
Behaves exactly like regular Squits, but with a health boost. It remains stationary until the Knight comes within range. Once engaged, it hovers a short distance away before flying directly at the Knight with its sharp proboscis raised. As it does not change direction during this charge, jumping or dashing over/through it is enough to avoid this attack.
Attacking an Armoured Squit mid-lunge changes its trajectory in the direction it is hit. They are most dangerous when grouped with other enemies, so it is best to take them out with one single hit of a Nail Art or Spell.
Location
Armoured Squits can be found in the Colosseum of Fools, in the Trial of the Conqueror and in the Trial of the Fool. Additionally, they can be spawned by the Collector in the  Hall of Gods on Ascended difficulty or above, and in the  Pantheon of Hallownest.
References
---

# 文档 [314] Aspid Hunter
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：aspid_hunter
- 路径：wiki/Aspid_Hunter

# Enemies：Aspid Hunter
**Aspid Hunters** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are the males of the Aspid species. Aspid Hunters usually hunt in packs and spit corrosive liquid at prey from a distance. A more powerful variant called Primal Aspids can be found in Kingdom's Edge.
Behaviour and Tactics
Aimlessly hovers around until approached by the Knight. It attacks from a distance by spitting blobs of corrosive liquid.
It is best to get in close and strike as soon as possible. They can easily be heard from a distance by the whirring sound their wings make.
Location
Aspid Hunters can be found in the Forgotten Crossroads (mainly the area where the Glowing Womb Charm is collected) and in the west side of the Ancient Basin Tram tunnel. They can also be spawned by the Collector.
Trivia
The Aspid Hunter is one of the few enemies that respawns upon leaving and re-entering the room.
In a Kickstarter update, it was referred to as **"Bulbous Hummingnit (Male)"**:
*"The male of this species is extremely aggressive, and will spit corrosive balls of venom at prey and intruders alike. Especially dangerous when encountered in packs."*
References

# 文档 [315] Aspid Mother
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：aspid_mother
- 路径：wiki/Aspid_Mother

# Enemies：Aspid Mother
**Aspid Mothers** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are the females of the Aspid species. Carrying their eggs inside their bodies, they can hatch and birth their young to attack threats.
Behaviour and Tactics
Births Aspid Hatchlings one at a time, up to a maximum of fifteen. Two more Hatchlings are spawned upon defeat.
The primary danger is that she can spawn many Aspid Hatchlings. Keep an eye on the Hatchlings and strike the mother either when there is an opening, or once the Hatchlings have been dealt with.
Location
Aspid Mothers can be found in the Forgotten Crossroads, mainly next to the Tram station.
Trivia
In a Kickstarter update, she was referred to as **"Bulbous Hummingnit (Female)"**:
*"The female of this species is just as aggressive as the male. Appallingly, it uses its own young as a defensive measure against intruders."*
A particularly large, dead Aspid Mother can be seen where the Glowing Womb Charm is collected, although she is not fought.
When Dream Nailed, she gives the line: *"Breed..."*
She is referred to as "giant_hatcher_corpse" and "HATCHLING_QUEEN_CORPSE" in the game files
Pre-release Aspid Mothers featured a reddish body colour rather than bright orange.
If an Aspid Mother has 14 or 15 Aspid Hatchlings spawned when killed, a large amount of Infection pours out instead of the usual two Hatchlings.
References

# 文档 [316] Battle Obble
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：battle_obble
- 路径：wiki/Battle_Obble

# Enemies：Battle Obble
**Battle Obbles** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. These bulbous creatures were raised in the Colosseum of Fools for combat. The Obble is their wild relative.
Behaviour and Tactics
Flies around in random patterns and intermittently fires four blobs of Infection in an X-shaped pattern. Also fires after taking any damage.
It does not directly target the Knight, but multiple spawn at once in the Colosseum, making dodging their shots difficult. The best strategy is to take them down quickly with a Nail Art or Spell (and possibly hit multiple at once). It is always recommended to stay beneath or directly beside this enemy, as its shots cannot hit the Knight.
They have far more health than regular Obbles; even a Great Slash from a Pure Nail fails to kill them in one hit.
Location
Battle Obbles are only found in the Colosseum of Fools, in the second and last Trials.
---

# 文档 [317] Bees
- 类别：lore
- 标识：bees
- 路径：wiki/Bees

# Lore：Bees
The lands of Hallownest are filled by several groups of strange sentient creatures. They occupy various territories around the vast kingdom and developed their own societies and cultures aside from the Pale King's rule.
**Table of Contents**
Bees • Flukes • Fools • Mantis Tribe • Mosskin Tribe • Moth Tribe • Mushroom Clan  • Snail Shamans • Soul Sanctum's Scholars • Spider Tribe • The Grimm Troupe • Godseekers
The residents of the Hive, below the Kingdom's Edge, are a species of sentient bees. These airborne warriors possess a hive mind which dictates their behaviour among the Hive. Hivelings carry out simple tasks, and can colonise husks to serve the Hive's purpose. Soldiers and Guardians defend the Hive against intruders. Lastly, the flightless but fierce  Hive Knight acts as the last rampart before their monarch, Hive Queen Vespa, who grew so huge she could not leave the Hive.
The Hive attacks any intruder who does not wield their blood. They also rejected the Pale King's attempt at perpetuation and separated themselves from the kingdom of Hallownest. Despite their isolation, Vespa's death weakened the Hive, allowing the Infection to spread through. The Infected residents never realised the death of their queen. Their corrupted hive mind dictated to defend her tirelessly, much to the sadness of their queen's spirit.
---

# 文档 [318] Bluggsac

- 标识：bluggsac

# Enemies：Bluggsac
**Bluggsacs** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are placid clusters of fluid sacs which occasionally produce a foul-smelling egg.
Behaviour and Tactics
Passive and stationary, it does not retaliate when attacked, nor does it deal contact damage. Drops a Rancid Egg upon death.
Location
They can be found scattered throughout Hallownest, with seemingly no pattern or main area of appearance.
1 in Blue Lake
2 in Crystal Peak
2 in Deepnest
1 in Kingdom's Edge
1 in Queen's Gardens
3 in Royal Waterways
Trivia
Bluggsacs are a source of infinite SOUL as they can be hit with the Dream Nail repeatedly.
They are not affected by environmental hazards and explosions.
The Bluggsac is one of the few enemies that never respawns.

# 文档 [319] Brooding Mawlek
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：brooding_mawlek
- 路径：wiki/Brooding_Mawlek

# Enemies：Brooding Mawlek
The **Brooding Mawlek** is a hidden boss in *Hollow Knight* as well as a Colosseum of Fools mini-boss.
In-game events
One lone Brooding Mawlek can be found off-road in the Forgotten Crossroads (or Infected Crossroads), far from its living brethren in the Ancient Basin. It sits amidst fossilised remains of its kind and calls for them to breed. This wild beast was driven mad both by its loneliness and the Infection which started covering its body with bulbs. It attacks the Knight as soon as they enter its room by jumping from the background. Upon defeat, the Infection bursts out of the Mawlek, making it explode.
Another one can be fought alone during one of the waves of the Trial of the Fool at the Colosseum. This Mawlek presents the same Infected state.
At the beginning of its fight in the Pantheon of Hallownest, Tiso appears instead as if entering a Trial. This only happens if he has been listened to in the Colosseum. He is then crushed by the Brooding Mawlek falling, which then engages the fight against the Knight.
Behaviour and Tactics
The Brooding Mawlek uses the following attacks:
**Slash**: Brooding Mawlek uses either of its claws to perform a downward slash towards the Knight. It only uses this attack if the Knight gets too close and can use it in conjunction with the Spit attack.
**Spit**: Brooding Mawlek spits blobs of Infection in parabolic arcs at regular intervals while skittering slowly across the ground. These blobs fly towards whichever side of the arena the Knight happens to be standing on. This attack can happen in conjunction with the Slash Attack. Brooding Mawlek spits 3-4 times before either performing a Leap or a Vomit.
**Leap**: Brooding Mawlek leaps to the Knight's location, landing where the Knight was at the beginning of its leap. Then, it immediately follows that leap with a jump back to the original position of where it landed at the start of the fight.
**Vomit**: Brooding Mawlek shoots a multitude of blobs of Infection in a parabolic arc simultaneously. These blobs fly towards whichever side of the arena the Knight happens to be standing on at the time. Brooding Mawlek stands idle until all the blobs have made contact with the ground.
Without the Longnail and Mark of Pride reach enhancing Charms, the Brooding Mawlek may retaliate when hit. A solid strategy is to hit it a few times and move away quickly when it raises its claw. It is also possible to jump over and Nail-bounce on it to get to the other side.
To dodge the Brooding Mawlek's leap, the Knight needs to run quickly in whichever direction they have space to move. This is also an opportunity to hit the Brooding Mawlek, which cannot Spit or Slash while in the air.
If the Knight has managed to obtain the Baldur Shell Charm and the Cyclone Slash Nail Art, it is possible to chip away at the Brooding Mawlek's health with the edge of Cyclone Slash and use the SOUL gained from the attack to heal safely inside Baldur Shell. While using Baldur Shell, the Knight can also enter into the body of the Brooding Mawlek without taking damage, allowing them to heal while it attacks.
When the Brooding Mawlek uses the Vomit attack, it is possible to safely dash over them with the Mothwing Cloak before the acid comes down. There are also some small safe spots in between the projectiles. It is also possible to Nail-bounce over to the other side.
If the Knight has the Sharp Shadow Charm, it can be used to dash through the Brooding Mawlek and deal damage.
Mark of Pride and Longnail make it easier to damage Brooding Mawlek when it performs the Slash attack while avoiding damage.
Another Brooding Mawlek is fought as part of the Trial of the Fool in the Colosseum of Fools in a very tight area where dodging its attacks is much more difficult.
Location
The Brooding Mawlek in the Forgotten Crossroads is found beyond a wall jump section in a blocked room to the left of the vertical shaft filled with Gruzzers and Tiktiks.
It is possible to reach by Nail-bouncing on the spikes, although it is recommended to have obtained the Mantis Claw instead.
Another Brooding Mawlek can be fought in the Colosseum of Fools as part of the Trial of the Fool.
Trivia
The Brooding Mawlek was the second mini-boss revealed in a Kickstarter update as an optional boss.
The Brooding Mawlek found in the Trial of the Fool is somewhat smaller and thinner than the one in Forgotten Crossroads. It has no behavioural differences.
This may be due to the size constraints of having a roof in the Colosseum.
Concept art of Brooding Mawlek under the name **"Vicious Mawlek"**, featured in a Team Cherry interview, shows it with extra sets of claws and teeth along its body.
---

# 文档 [320] Carver Hatcher

# Enemies：Carver Hatcher
**Carver Hatchers** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are flying creatures who spawn Dirtcarvers when prey is nearby.
Behaviour and Tactics
Spawns Dirtcarvers while hovering above the Knight, tries to back away and evade when the Knight gets close.
It is best to take care of this enemy first in a fight, as otherwise, it continues to spawn enemies and makes the fight more difficult.
After spawning five Dirtcarvers, it starts swooping and chasing the Knight to bite them. While doing so it starts to emit a gurgling sound.
Location
Carver Hatchers can only be spotted in the north part of Deepnest, where the Failed Tramway is located.

# 文档 [322] City Crest
- 类别：items
- 标识：city_crest
- 路径：wiki/City_Crest

# Items：City Crest
The **City Crest** is an Item in *Hollow Knight*.
Use
Opens the gate between the Fungal Wastes and the City of Tears. The Mantis Claw is required to gain access to this area of the Fungal Wastes.
The Crest needs to be inserted into a slot on a statue of the Great Knight Hegemol. Placing it there consumes the City Crest.
After walking through the opened gate, it closes and cannot be opened again. It is possible to open the ceiling above the gate by coming from the City of Tears and using the Desolate Dive/Descending Dark Spell on a breakable floor.
While the intended entrance to the City of Tears is to use the City Crest, there are additional ways to enter the City of Tears, such as dropping down from the Resting Grounds or coming from the Royal Waterways.
How to Acquire
Drops from False Knight in the Forgotten Crossroads after defeating him.
---

# 文档 [324] Cowardly Husk

# Enemies：Cowardly Husk
**Cowardly Husks** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. These reanimated bugs used to belong to Hallownest's high society, and their cowardly nature still persists after death.
Behaviour and Tactics
Meanders back and forth. When disturbed, it either runs towards the Knight and deals contact damage or flees. If backed into a corner, either the edge of an area or against a solid wall, it may occasionally fall into pits and drown rather than run towards the Knight.
Location
They are located in the east part of the City of Tears, much like the Husk Dandy. There is one in the top of the Watcher's Spire.
Trivia
