# 文档 [362] Seals
- 类别：lore
- 标识：seals
- 路径：wiki/Seals

# Lore：Seals
**Seals** are magical formations which appear in both Hallownest and Pharloom. They have various functions and features.
Characteristics
Appearance
Seals are white-glowing formations which consist of interconnected lines and geometric shapes. Some seals contain stylised imagery of certain characters such as the Hollow Knight. Most seals do not automatically appear but require certain actions before they are revealed, such as attacking an object or a character.
Function
Several seals are shown to protect living beings or inanimate objects from damage. Seals might also exist to block access to certain areas or to trap somebody in a specific place. The only named seal, the  Seal of Binding, is used to contain a powerful force or preserve something of great importance. In some cases it is unknown what the function of a specific seal is.
History
Hallownest
Seals play a major role in Hallownest's history. The seals of the Dreamers were part of the Pale King's plan to seal the Radiance away. Three powerful bugs were chosen to enter an eternal sleep. They became seals on the entrance to the Black Egg to protect the Hollow Knight inside.
When the Infection returned and the Hollow Knight weakened, the Dreamers' seals still remained. Their seals can only be broken if their minds are accessed and they are killed inside their dream.
Pharloom
Hornet was taken to Pharloom in a cage by bugs of the Citadel's caste. This cage was protected by a seal. At some point in the journey, a white flying bug appeared which landed on the cage and broke the seal. The mask on the door starts shaking and the seal is shown flickering. The seal then flashes in a bright flash of light and disappears along with the lit-up mask on Black Egg.
|
|-
! colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|Dreamer shrine seals
|-
|
When first approaching the Dreamer shrine in the Resting Grounds, these seals appear around the shrine, blocking the way out. After the Dreamers send the Knight into a forgotten dream and the Dream Nail is obtained, these seals no longer show up.
|
|-
! colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"| Pure Vessel arena seals
|-
|
These seals appear on the sides of Pure Vessel's arena, where they prevent leaving the arena. They consist of two types of overlapping seals which show up when approaching the sides. The wider seal appears first after coming closer to the edge, then the thinner seal appears over this seal when standing right next to the edge. The seals can be wall climbed on.
|
Damage protection seals
Seals which protect somebody from being damaged by physical weapons or Spells.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|Dreamers' physical body seals
The seals on the Dreamers' physical bodies partially appear when approaching their bodies. They show up fully when their bodies are attacked with either Spells or Nail strikes. After the Dreamers are killed in their dream, these seals no longer appear.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|The Hollow Knight  seal
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|White Lady  seal
Seal of Binding
The Seal of Binding is an intricate seal of ancient design and the only named seal in Hallownest. Its main distinctive feature is the stylised head of the Hollow Knight at the top of the seal. In its Hunter's Journal entry, this seal is described as being used to contain a powerful force, or to preserve something of great importance.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"| Path of Pain
The full version of the Seal of Binding is shown at the entrance to the Path of Pain. The Hunter's Journal entry of the Seal of Binding is granted at the end of the Path of Pain.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|Sideways version
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|Weavers' Den
Miscellaneous seals
Seals which do not fit into any other section.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|Beast's Den shrine seal
A seal is shown when using a Spell on the being in Beast's Den. The sprites in this room contain the word "shrine" in their name. It is unknown what the purpose of the seal is.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|Hornet cage seal
There is a seal on Hornet's cage in which she was taken to Pharloom. A small flying bug breaks this seal, after which Hornet ends up escaping.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|King's Brand seal
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"| Path of Pain Kingsmould room seal
Possible seals
The following formations do not look anything like the other seal designs. They may be seals, but this has not been confirmed.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|Essence seal
This seal is shown when using the unawoken Dream Nail on the Kingsmould corpse in the Palace Grounds. It also shows up on the Dreamers in their dreams. It fades away after approaching the Dreamer.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"| Grimm seal
When Troupe Master Grimm is sleeping and Grimmchild is equipped, he can be Dream Nailed to start the fight with Nightmare King Grimm. If he is Dream Nailed without having Grimmchild equipped, a seal shows up which consists of red Essence.

# 文档 [363] Shielded Fool
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：shielded_fool
- 路径：wiki/Shielded_Fool

# Enemies：Shielded Fool
**Shielded Fools** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are shielded combatants who fight for glory in the Colosseum of Fools.
Behaviour and Tactics
Cautiously walks towards the Knight, raising its shield when they come close, which blocks any damage from the front (except for Spells). If the Knight moves too close, they may back off a few steps.
After taking a hit to the shield, or waiting long enough with the Knight in front of them, they lunge forward followed by a slash. Occasionally they lunge and slash a second time. Their attacks are very telegraphed and can be dodged easily; the second swing is only slightly faster than the first one. Bait them into attacking, then counter-attack while they recover or jump over/dash through them and hit them from behind. When the Knight jumps above them while they are not attacking, they use their shield to protect themselves from above.
Alternatively, since they only raise their shield at a certain distance, ranged attacks such as Vengeful Spirit/Shade Soul, the Grubberfly's Elegy Charm, and even the Dash Slash Nail Art can be used to dispose of them easily.
Using the Dream Nail on the Shielded Fool is a good way to gain full SOUL, especially when combined with the Dream Wielder Charm. This is especially useful in the Trial of the Fool, where it is easy to take lots of damage. This is good for reaching God Tamer with full SOUL and full health. It is recommended to save the Shielded Fool as the last enemy alive to attempt this.
Location
This enemy is only found in the Colosseum of Fools, in all of the three trials.
References
---

# 文档 [365] Simple Key
- 类别：items
- 标识：simple_key
- 路径：wiki/Simple_Key

# Items：Simple Key
**Simple Keys** are Items in *Hollow Knight*. They can be used to open simple locks. Each key can only be used once.
Use
There are 4  locations that can be opened using Simple Keys:
The entrance to the Royal Waterways from the City of Tears.
The cave to the right of Dirtmouth, beyond the graveyard. This cave is home to Confessor Jiji, who, in return for a Rancid Egg, can summon the Knight's Shade, which is useful if the Shade is stuck in a hard-to-access area and holding a lot of Geo. In Steel Soul Mode, the cave is instead home to Steel Soul Jinn, who trades Rancid Eggs from the Knight for Geo.
The Pleasure House in the City of Tears, along with a Hot Spring, Poggy Thorax, and Songstress Marissa. It is also Millibelle's refuge after she scams the Knight. Once inside, a shortcut can be opened from the Hot Spring to a lift shaft that leads from the City of Tears to the Resting Grounds, and also grants easy access to the northern part of Kingdom's Edge and the Colosseum of Fools.
The cocoon of the Godseeker in the Junk Pit. Using the Dream Nail on her grants access to Godhome.
How to Acquire
One can be bought from Sly in Dirtmouth for .
Shop description:
*Simply, a Simple key. It will fit a variety of locks, which is useful if you like to poke around in places you don't belong.*
One can be found in the City of Tears, in the big room with Winged Sentries and a Whispering Root just below the City Storerooms. The key is located in the topmost alcove on the right of the room.
One can be found in the Ancient Basin, on the dead body of a Royal Retainer inside a Mawlurk corpse.
One can be obtained by killing the Pale Lurker in a hidden area behind the Colosseum of Fools.
Trivia
The sprite for the Simple Key is called the "graveyard key" and both a "Bath house key" and "Waterways key" exist in the game files implying that Jiji/Jinn's cave, the Pleasure House, and the Royal Waterways were each originally planned to be opened by these unique keys.
---

# 文档 [366] Snail Shamans
- 类别：lore
- 标识：snail_shamans
- 路径：wiki/Snail_Shamans

# Lore：Snail Shamans
The lands of Hallownest are filled by several groups of strange sentient creatures. They occupy various territories around the vast kingdom and developed their own societies and cultures aside from the Pale King's rule.
**Table of Contents**
Bees • Flukes • Fools • Mantis Tribe • Mosskin Tribe • Moth Tribe • Mushroom Clan  • Snail Shamans • Soul Sanctum's Scholars • Spider Tribe • The Grimm Troupe • Godseekers
The **Snail Shamans** are a mysterious tribe of snail creatures with a natural affinity to cast Soul Spells. Their knowledge of Soul allows them to craft Charms such as Soul Catcher, Soul Eater, and Shaman Stone to draw Soul from still-living creatures and increase the power of Spells. Because of these abilities, one of them was captured by the Scholars of the Soul Sanctum and experimented on. They can also sense when their dreams are read with a Dream Nail, and absorbing their remains allows the Knight to upgrade their Spells. Their abilities with Soul also include a "Spiral Focus", though what this truly is, is unknown.
The shamans are reclusive, and meditate in mounds hidden away in the Forgotten Crossroads, the Fog Canyon and the Crystal Peak. They also have a crypt in the catacombs below the Resting Grounds. They however never ventured down the Abyss, despite its connection to the civilisation that left Soul Totems scattered throughout Hallownest.
Only one of them can be found alive by the time of the Knight's journey. While he is eager to help those seeking him out, he is unaware of the fate of his brethren and family, being bound to his mound. The shamans' power is also stated to be shunned; possibly by the kingdom of Hallownest, though it is unclear why.
---

# 文档 [367] Soul Sanctum's Scholars
- 类别：lore
- 标识：soul_sanctums_scholars
- 路径：wiki/Soul_Sanctum's_Scholars

# Lore：Soul Sanctum's Scholars
The lands of Hallownest are filled by several groups of strange sentient creatures. They occupy various territories around the vast kingdom and developed their own societies and cultures aside from the Pale King's rule.
**Table of Contents**
Bees • Flukes • Fools • Mantis Tribe • Mosskin Tribe • Moth Tribe • Mushroom Clan  • Snail Shamans • Soul Sanctum's Scholars • Spider Tribe • The Grimm Troupe • Godseekers
The bugs of the Soul Sanctum are highly intelligent scholars who served the Kingdom of Hallownest. They researched ways to expand the mind and attain pure focus, secluded in their Sanctum in the kingdom's capital. When the kingdom's minds became plagued by the Infection, the Soul Master, head of the Sanctum, sought its cure in Soul, the energy animating bugs and beasts alike. He refused to listen to the Pale King opposing his work,
In their madness, the scholars consumed souls, convinced it would lead them to immortality. These experiments had their share of failures, deforming some of them into formless Mistakes and Follies. More successful ones retained their physical integrity, becoming supernaturally skilled Soul Twisters and Soul Warriors.
The Infected scholars kept hoarding souls as the Kingdom fell. They gathered Soul Totems and many bugs from which to harvest the vital energy. They eventually used the furthest rooms of the Sanctum to unceremoniously discard the ancient structures as well as the husks of their victims. They even captured a Snail Shaman to forcefully steal its Soul abilities.
Unlike the kingdom's bugs, the scholars survived the fall of Hallownest. Some of them remain in the Soul Sanctum and attack any intruder, with the Soul Master still clinging to the Infection's false promise of immortality. Others, although also Infected, joined the Colosseum of Fools as fighters. The Volt Twisters, in particular, adopted the teachings of the Sanctum to evolve their abilities and continue fighting or meditating in seclusion.
Trivia
An early concept sketch shows a scholar with growths of Infection on their body.
---

# 文档 [368] Soul Twister
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：soul_twister
- 路径：wiki/Soul_Twister

# Enemies：Soul Twister
Not to be confused with Spell Twister.
**Soul Twisters** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are scholars of the Soul Sanctum who have learnt how to harness the power of SOUL, which they twist into spells and use to teleport.
Behaviour and Tactics
Appearing out of thin air upon entering their territory, a Soul Twister either conjures an orb to protect itself, or already has an orb upon teleporting into battle. Afterwards, it pursues the Knight by teleporting and conjuring homing offensive orbs to attack with. It teleports frequently around its territory, making it difficult to hit and impossible to corner. It hovers a certain distance away from the Knight at all times, though it must remain stationary to conjure an orb. If the Knight enters an area it cannot teleport to, it teleports out of the vicinity but returns once the Knight re-enters its territory and resumes the battle.
It is recommended to use Nail Arts such as Great Slash to dispatch them quickly. Dash Slash can also help close the range with them.
If neither of these options are available, the best tactic then is to wait for the Soul Twister to conjure an offensive orb and then rush in to attack it after avoiding its projectile, as it cannot teleport immediately after firing a projectile. Depending on its location, avoiding the orb can be as simple as jumping over or dashing. Utilizing the terrain to prevent them from attacking from disadvantageous positions is also advised. Forcing them into smaller rooms and hallways where they have fewer angles of attack is also recommended to make dodging more predictable, and to make it easier to get in hits. Vengeful Spirit/Shade Soul is also useful for attacking at range, as they do not deliberately teleport to avoid projectiles.
Fleeing from these enemies is very difficult, as they relentlessly teleport after the Knight upon their activation. However, they do not follow the Knight into other rooms marked via a screen transition.
Location
They appear in the Soul Sanctum, only to the east of the Soul Master arena. They also appear in the 9th, 10th, 11th and 17th waves of the Trial of the Fool.
References
---

# 文档 [369] Spider Tribe
- 类别：lore
- 标识：spider_tribe
- 路径：wiki/Spider_Tribe

# Lore：Spider Tribe
The lands of Hallownest are filled by several groups of strange sentient creatures. They occupy various territories around the vast kingdom and developed their own societies and cultures aside from the Pale King's rule.
**Table of Contents**
Bees • Flukes • Fools • Mantis Tribe • Mosskin Tribe • Moth Tribe • Mushroom Clan  • Snail Shamans • Soul Sanctum's Scholars • Spider Tribe • The Grimm Troupe • Godseekers
The beasts of Deepnest are arachnids in appearance and used to be one of the most intelligent species in the land of Hallownest. Unlike the Pale King's Kingdom, the Nest was not led by a king of honoured caste, but a queen of common descent, Herrah the Beast. She outlived her consort but her followers, Little Weavers, Stalking Devouts and Weavers, continued serving both their queen and the Nest with devotion.
The creatures of the Nest lived in the Distant Village, houses of silk suspended in a deep cavern at the far end of Deepnest. Their brood was tended to by creatures such as Midwife, were not natives of Hallownest and resided in their own den, hidden at the heart of Deepnest.
The Nest kept their territory bound at the edge of Deepnest and defended it with hostility against the Fungal Tribe. such as by violently forcing the Kingdom to cease the construction of a tram line throughout the upper part of their territory. The Mantis Tribe kept the Nest's beasts from pushing further, following a truce with the Kingdom.
Eventually, the Pale King was able to bargain with Herrah the Beast for her help in containing the Infection plaguing Hallownest. The Distant Village was also linked to the kingdom's Stagways, although its station was never visited by the Last Stag before the Knight's journey. With her consort dead, In exchange, the queen became a Dreamer to seal the Hollow Knight, the Vessel containing the Infection. Yet, this sacrifice proved unsuccessful and the Nest found itself Infected nonetheless. but would eventually return, seeking answers throughout the doomed land of Hallownest. The Weavers also left Deepnest to return to their old home outside Hallownest. Herrah's surviving followers continue to protect her by hunting intruders, their mind clouded by the Infection. The Distant Village itself grew silent, with the exception of the Beast's Den serving as a deadly trap for unfortunate wanderers.
---

# 文档 [370] Stalking Devout
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：stalking_devout
- 路径：wiki/Stalking_Devout

# Enemies：Stalking Devout
**Stalking Devouts** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They are cloaked worshippers of Herrah the Beast who use their foreclaws to shield their head.
Behaviour and Tactics
Found in narrow tunnels, sleeping. Upon engaging, it skitters back and forth, often waiting in one spot before moving again or attacking. It is invulnerable from the front unless it is attacking.
If its foreclaws are hit, it immediately retaliates. To attack, it opens its foreclaws, exposing its face for a moment before leaping forward in a flurry of attacks that deal 2 Masks of damage. Strike it when it is exposed and quickly dash away from its attacks.
When approached from behind, it does not attack unless hit. This provides a good opportunity to hit it with a Nail Art or a Spell or to use the Dream Nail to get SOUL.
It has no retaliation against attacking from above, so if possible, lure it into a more open room and Nail-bounce on it until dead. Using the Great Slash Nail Art on its foreclaws hits twice, once to open it, and one tick of damage while it is vulnerable; be sure to dash away immediately after the second hit to avoid damage. The same method can be used with Dash Slash from certain ranges, allowing a little more distance to be kept from the creature.
Another method to defeat it is to get close to it so that it opens its foreclaws to attack and then quickly swipe at its face before dashing away as it begin its attack sequence. This is the simplest and most risk-free way, but it takes a fairly long time to kill it. However, combining the Sharp Shadow Charm into this tactic can hasten the killing process by simply dashing through it instead of away from it whenever it attempts to attack. If fast enough, striking it again with the Nail immediately after dashing through is possible, making killing it even shorter.
Location
The Stalking Devout can be rarely seen in the west part of Deepnest and Distant Village.
Trivia
The Stalking Devout guarding Herrah's chamber disappears forever after Herrah has been killed.
References
---

# 文档 [371] Tram Pass

# Items：Tram Pass
The **Tram Pass** is an Item in *Hollow Knight*.
Use
Allows the Knight to ride the Tram. If the Tram is inspected before acquiring the pass, the description reads "A door with an open slot."
How to Acquire
Found in the Failed Tramway in Deepnest in the wreck of a tram.
Trivia
After acquiring the pass, the Last Stag comments on it, saying:
*"That pass you hold! Is it not for that ghastly machine, the tram? I hope you're not thinking of riding on that grotesque contraption.*
*The thought a mere machine could attempt what we stags do! Foolish...Very foolish."*

# 文档 [372] Vengefly King
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：vengefly_king
- 路径：wiki/Vengefly_King

# Enemies：Vengefly King
The **Vengefly King** is an optional mini-boss in *Hollow Knight* as well as a Colosseum of Fools mini-boss. Unlocking its Journal entry requires defeating 2 Vengefly Kings.
In-game events
Vengefly Kings are the territorial patriarchs of Vengeflies and are native to Greenpath. One can be encountered above the roads of Greenpath, hanging on the ceiling and chewing on Zote. Harming it prompts it to release Zote and fight the Knight. Upon defeat, the Infection bursts out of it and makes it explode. Neglecting to help Zote results instead in the Vengefly King eating him before disappearing.
One more Vengefly King can be fought during the Trial of the Warrior.
Behaviour & Tactics
The Vengefly King has two attacks:
**Swipe**: The Vengefly King opens its jaw and swoops at the Knight in a wide 'U' shape.
**Summoning Scream**: The Vengefly King emits a screech, summoning between 0 and 2 Vengeflies. A maximum of 4 Vengeflies can be alive at once.
If it opens its mouth to Swipe, wait until it starts moving and jump over it as it approaches. Either perform a downward slash to get in some damage or simply avoid it.
When it summons normal Vengeflies, it is best to kill them as quickly as possible. The longer they are around, the more difficult dodging the Vengefly King becomes, especially when it summons more Vengeflies. The Vengeflies provide an easy way to get SOUL.
There is enough time to heal immediately after dodging a Swipe attack.
Location
The Vengefly King is first encountered in the northern part of Greenpath. It can also be fought in the Trial of the Warrior at the Colosseum of Fools.
Achievements
Trivia
If Zote is not rescued, then the Vengefly King in Greenpath cannot be fought. However, the Hunter's Journal entry can still be completed when one is fought in the Trial of the Warrior or in  Godhome.
Despite having an unlock text in the  Hall of Gods, it is impossible to see it in-game as Vengefly King's statue is automatically unlocked.
References
---

# 文档 [373] Vessel Fragment
- 类别：items
- 标识：vessel_fragment
- 路径：wiki/Vessel_Fragment

# Items：Vessel Fragment
**Vessel Fragments** are Items in *Hollow Knight* that increase the Knight's maximum SOUL.
Use
Vessel Fragments are parts of Soul Vessels. 3 Vessel Fragments complete a Soul Vessel and increases the Knight's maximum SOUL by 33. When the main Soul meter has empty space, any SOUL stored in the Vessels will automatically fill up the main meter after a short delay.
The Nail acquires SOUL for the Soul Vessels at a reduced rate, only providing 6 SOUL.
The Soul Catcher Charm increases this to 8 SOUL.
The Soul Eater Charm increases this to 12 SOUL.
These effects stack, giving 14 SOUL if both are equipped.
All other sources of SOUL do not fill Soul Vessels at a reduced rate, instead filling them at their normal rate.
With a total of 9 Vessel Fragments in the game, 3 Soul Vessels can be acquired, doubling the maximum amount of SOUL that can be carried to 198.
How to Acquire
There are a total of 9 Vessel Fragments to be found in the game:

Trivia
While the fountain in the Ancient Basin will always ask "Drop all Geo into the fountain?", only a total of  will be added. Any extra will not be subtracted.
The music heard after acquiring three Vessel Fragments originates from a short sample track that was posted when Christopher Larkin was hired as the game's composer.
There are unused sprites found in the game files which suggest that a Soul Vessel originally consisted of only two Vessel Fragments, showing two halves which needed to be collected to acquire a full Soul Vessel. The "Ferocious Foes" trailer also shows Sly selling one half of a Soul Vessel. This was changed to three fragments for the final release.
This might be why Sly still refers to his two Vessel Fragments as being a complete set.
This also explains why the statue of the Pale King by the fountain in the Ancient Basin is holding half of a Soul Vessel, instead of a third.

# 文档 [374] Vessels
- 类别：lore
- 标识：vessels
- 路径：wiki/Vessels

# Lore：Vessels
**Vessels** are genderless beings of the Void who were created by the Pale King as a means of stopping the Infection. They are described as the progeny of the Pale King and the spawn of the White Lady, containing the "soul" of the two beings. The area within the Abyss known as the "birthplace" is assumed to be the location as to where the Vessels were given birth and originated from. This area is where most of them were discarded following the Pale King’s search for a Pure Vessel.
Eventually, one Vessel was judged to be pure and was chosen to seal the Radiance within themself. This Vessel was named the Hollow Knight.
During the birthplace cutscene, the following dialogue is presented:
No mind to think.
No will to break.
No voice to cry suffering.
Born of God and Void.
This dialogue comes from Pale King and appears to be referring to the Hollow Knight - also present at the top of the Abyss aside the Pale King himself.
The Siblings found at the bottom of the Abyss are implied to be the Shades that originate from the shells of deceased Vessels. From this enemy and the Lost Kin boss, it can be interpreted that all Vessels are siblings. Hornet calls the Hollow Knight the sibling of both her and of the Knight, also suggesting a sibling relationship. Furthermore, the achievement unlocked after defeating the Hollow Knight with Voidheart is called Sealed Siblings.
After the Hollow Knight was lead out of the Abyss, the Pale King sealed the Abyss with a seal that could only be broken by somebody with the King's Brand, locking most of the other Vessels inside. Other Vessels can be found scattered across the world and the Knight starts their journey outside of the Abyss in Howling Cliffs. This suggests that despite being locked away, some Vessels still managed to find a method to escape.
List of Vessels
colspan="2" |
width="70%" | The Knight is the Vessel that the player controls throughout the game. They escaped the Abyss and wandered outside of Hallownest for unknown reasons. The Dreamers suggest that they only returned to Hallownest after a call from either the Radiance or the Hollow Knight.
colspan="2" |
The Hollow Knight, as they are referred to on the Abyss entrance Lore Tablet, is the Vessel chosen by the Pale King with the task to seal the Radiance. They are also known as "Pure Vessel" or simply "the Vessel". Unlike most of their siblings, the Hollow Knight is said to be fully-grown. Although they were thought to be a pure Vessel, they were ultimately unable to contain the Infection forever, which lead to the events of Hollow Knight (game). A younger version of the Hollow Knight is seen in a cutscene at the end of Path of Pain.
colspan="2" |
The Broken Vessel (and its Dream variant, the Lost Kin) is a hollowed-out shell of a fallen Vessel found in the Ancient Basin reanimated by Lightseeds. The Infection drove it mad but also made it stronger. It still carries many of the skills it possessed.
colspan="2" |
This Vessel's body is found in Greenpath, in the same area that Hornet is located in when she first fights the Knight. They are equipped with the Mothwing Cloak which is passed on to the Knight once their corpse is inspected after defeating her.
colspan="2" |
Nosk's arena in Deepnest has several Vessel corpses hung up in the background. These Vessels escaped the Abyss and somehow ended up in Deepnest.
colspan="2" |
A large portion of the ground of the Abyss is covered in the shells of dead Vessels - particularly the whole of the birthplace area seems to be composed entirely of Vessel shells. They are shown to fall from the top of the Abyss in the scene before the Knight acquires the Void Heart Charm.
colspan="2" |
The scene that is shown after the Knight defeats Pure Vessel in the Pantheon of the Knight depicts numerous Vessels in front and behind the Knight and the young Hollow Knight. The setting seems to take place in the Abyss.
Trivia
On the east end of the Birthplace, which is located at the bottom of the Abyss, is an egg with Void tendrils attached to it. This may imply that the Void possessed and hollowed out the vessels before they had even hatched from their eggs.
Despite common belief, Hornet isn't a Vessel nor Void, as she was never hollowed out in the abyss, and is thus called the gendered child.
While all Vessels wear cloaks, those infected by the Radiance's cloaks are severely discoloured compared to those still filled with void, in the Abyss and even on the Knight.
---

# 文档 [375] Void
- 类别：lore
- 标识：void
- 路径：wiki/Void

# Lore：Void
**Void** is a substance that is generally found in the Abyss. It plays a major role in Hallownest's history and in current events.
**Table of Contents**
Characteristics • History • In-game events • Void beings
Characteristics
Nature
Void inherently opposes light and is often referred to as darkness and shadow. It also opposes Higher Beings like the Radiance and the Pale King who are both described as a light.
Void has a certain potential when it is unified. When not unified, the Void attacks anything indiscriminately. Yet in this state, the Void can still be suppressed by light sources such as a lighthouse filled with lumaflies.
Once the Void is united under one will, it no longer attacks aimlessly and can instead challenge and defeat the source of the Infection.
States
Void exists primarily in two states, as a liquid and as a substance given form. The largest amount of liquid Void is the sea of Void at the bottom of the Abyss. When the Void is not unified and when light does not shine upon the liquid in the Abyss, it lashes out with sharp tendrils towards intruders. Void can also take a form within the shell or armour of life forms, which is the case for the Vessels, the Kingsmoulds, and the Wingmoulds, who have an interior filled with Void.
Outside of life forms, Void can take the shape of a Shade Gate, which is a barrier that consists of Void.
Influence
Void has an effect on living beings and on certain objects. The sea of Void called to the lighthouse keeper in the Abyss to turn off the light. It also appears to have killed various bugs found throughout Ancient Basin and the bug which holds the Love Key in the Queen's Gardens, who all have Void leaking from their eyes.
The Soul Totem upon which the Sharp Shadow Charm is found seems to have been corrupted by Void. It has Void tendrils attached to it, and the totem itself has become darker in colour. The egg found in the Birthplace area in the Abyss similarly has Void tendrils connected to it.
History
Ancient times
In the distant past, the Void used to be worshipped by an ancient civilisation. It is not known whether there was an actual conflict between the two or during which time they became enemies.
Arrival of the Pale King
Sometime after the Pale King arrived in Hallownest, he discovered the Void in the Abyss. He built a lighthouse on top of a natural spire near the sea of Void which was used to suppress the Void. The Pale King took Void from the sea and used it in his workshop in the White Palace to create constructs that have Void within them, the Kingsmoulds and Wingmoulds.
The Pale King chose one of these children, the Hollow Knight, to be the Vessel that would seal the Radiance inside themself.
In-game events
Void Heart
After remembering their past and accepting the Void inside themself, the Knight obtains Void Heart. Void Heart allows them to unite the Void under their will. The Knight is then also referred to as "Lord of Shades". Void Heart causes the Void Tendrils and the Siblings in the Abyss to become passive, as well as the Knight's own Shade.
Dream No More ending
In the Dream No More ending, the Knight pulls the Void and the Siblings into the fight with the Radiance. At the end of the fight, tendrils of Void grab the Radiance, after which the Shade of the Hollow Knight opens a weak spot on the Radiance's face.
The Knight then breaks their shell and attacks the Radiance in their Shade form. The Radiance is subsequently pulled into the Void and consumed by it. Finally, the Shades in the Abyss are seen going back inside the ground.
 Embrace the Void endings
In Godhome, Void Heart is required to enter the Pantheon of Hallownest. Inside this Pantheon, the Knight pulls the Void into the fight with the Absolute Radiance, similar to how it plays out with the regular Radiance. However, the Siblings are nowhere to be seen during the fight.
At the end of the fight, the Knight turns into the Void Entity. This being grabs the Absolute Radiance and completely destroys her, making her explode into Essence. Void is shown streaming downwards into the area where Godseeker was observing the fight. The Void Entity moves towards Godseeker and wraps tendrils around her.
If a Delicate Flower was not given to Godseeker, Void leaks from her body in the Junk Pit. Tendrils then appear to burst from her body, after which the scene ends. If a Delicate Flower was given to her, Void tendrils similarly explode from her body, but a white flash appears from the flower. Godseeker and the Void disappear, leaving only the Flower behind.
Void beings with exterior
The following is a list of Void beings who have a shell or armour and Void within that.
colspan="2" class="typography--headline6"|Kingsmoulds
Kingsmoulds are Void constructs with white armour made by the Pale King in his workshop in the White Palace.
colspan="2"  class="typography--headline6"|Siblings/Shade
The Knight's Shade and the Siblings are the Void forms that exist inside Vessels. The Shade is let loose after a Vessel's shell breaks. Many roam the bottom of the Abyss and the Birthplace area.
colspan="2"  class="typography--headline6"| Void given Focus
Also known as "Shade Lord" in the game's files, Void given Focus is a colossal being of pure Void that the Knight transforms into upon completing the Pantheon of Hallownest. Referred to as "God of Gods" by Godseeker.
colspan="2"  class="typography--headline6"|Void given Form
The Knight transforms into this being upon defeating the Radiance in the Temple of the Black Egg. It resembles the Knight's Shade but with longer tendrils emanating from it.
colspan="2"  class="typography--headline6"|Void Tendrils
Void Tendrils are fragments of Void that are found in pools in the Abyss and in the sea of Void. An imprint of them can be found engraved into a rock in the Abyss.
---

# 文档 [376] Volt Twister
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：volt_twister
- 路径：wiki/Volt_Twister

# Enemies：Volt Twister
**Volt Twisters** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. They were scholars of Soul Sanctum who attack using bursts of electricity. They spend their entire lives fighting in the Colosseum of Fools or meditating alone.
Behaviour and Tactics
Volt Twisters teleport around the area, attempting to avoid the Knight. They have only one attack, which consists of them charging up and releasing a series of 8 electric bursts of lightning that spawn at the Knight's location, very similar to one of Uumuu's attacks.
A Volt Twister is most vulnerable during its attack since it remains completely stationary while casting and for a short time afterwards. It is recommended to either attack it with ranged abilities or to charge-up a Nail Art, let it its attack end, and then move in close for the attack.
Location
This enemy is only found in the Colosseum of Fools, in the Trial of the Fool.
References
---

# 文档 [377] Wanderer's Journal
- 类别：items
- 标识：wanderers_journal
- 路径：wiki/Wanderer's_Journal

# Items：Wanderer's Journal
**Wanderer's Journals** are tablets found commonly throughout Hallownest. They are always found next to corpses that are assumed to be the authors of the journal.
What is written on them is unknown as they can not be read and are said to be written in different languages, but Relic Seeker Lemm proclaims his ability to decipher the text.
While the City of Tears ended up using parchment woven of spider's silk, the wanderer's journals are of traditional stone type upon which text endures well.
Uses
Can be sold to Relic Seeker Lemm for .
Shop description:
These journals give us an interesting glimpse into the minds and hearts of those who lived before us.
They're a common find, so I can't offer you too much for them.
How to Acquire
There are a total of 14 Wanderer's Journals that can be obtained:
2 found in Greenpath.
1 outside of the Stag Station behind a breakable wall.
1 in the room connecting to Fog Canyon.
2 found in Fungal Wastes.
1 in the room southwest of where two Shrumal Ogres are encountered.
1 near the Whispering Root above the Mantis Village.
3 found in the City of Tears.
1 to the west of the City Storerooms Stag Station.
1 in the room above King's Station.
1 in the Pleasure House behind a hidden passage.
1 found in the Howling Cliffs behind a breakable wall.
1 found in Crystal Peak in a room with 7 Crystal Crawlers.
1 found in the Resting Grounds in a room near the Soul Eater Charm.
1 found in the Royal Waterways in the room which connects to Ancient Basin.
3 found in Kingdom's Edge.
1 in the western part near the entrance to King's Station.
1 next to the Bench on the path leading to the Cast-Off Shell.
1 beneath a dive floor in the room before Markoth.
References

# 文档 [378] Wandering Husk

- 标识：wandering_husk
- 路径：wiki/Wandering_Husk

# Enemies：Wandering Husk
**Wandering Husks** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. Once citizens of Hallownest, these reanimated corpses now wander the roads of the kingdom.
Behaviour and Tactics
Meanders back and forth until disturbed. It then flails its arms about wildly and runs at the Knight, dealing contact damage.
Location
They can be found in large quantities in the Forgotten Crossroads, though only one can be found there after they become Infected. They can also be found in Greenpath, the City of Tears, and Deepnest.
Trivia
In a Kickstarter update, it was referred to as **"Endemons Sapien (Infected)"**:
*"These vicious, mindless ghouls were once ordinary bugs like you and me. Something below the surface has burnt away their souls and filled them with an aimless rage."*

# 文档 [379] Weavers
- 类别：lore
- 标识：weavers
- 路径：wiki/Weavers

# Lore：Weavers
The **Weavers** are a tribe of spiders that originate from Pharloom. They used to reside deep in the recesses of Deepnest in their own den. Despite bearing resemblance to the other creatures in Deepnest, such as the Deepling, they came from outside of Hallownest and established their own history and culture in Deepnest.
The weavers once crafted stories, shields, and spells on their looms. The  Weaversong Charm is a remnant of what the Weavers could create with their talents. In the Weavers' Den, a seal can be found which is almost identical to the  Seal of Binding seen in the  Path of Pain.
The tribe left Hallownest and returned to their old home
Trivia
The Weavers were originally supposed to appear in the game as a regular enemy early in development, but did not make the cut in the long run for unknown reasons. They were referred to as a **Spider Mage** and would lurk in the darkest corners of Hallownest.
There is a Weaver wrapped up in webs seen in the *Hollow Knight: Silksong* trailer.
The only known living Weavers are the Weaver found in Weaver's Den, the Widow, Hornet and the First Sinner.
---

# 文档 [380] Winged Fool
- 类别：enemies
- 标识：winged_fool
- 路径：wiki/Winged_Fool

# Enemies：Winged Fool
**Winged Fools** are enemies in *Hollow Knight*. These winged warriors fight other bugs to the death in the Colosseum of Fools.
Behaviour and Tactics
They hover outside of the Knight's reach, then lunge toward them in an arc, slashing their weapon.
This pattern is easy to predict and follow, simply jump over the attack or dash through it and hit them on the recovery. They can also be defeated by using the Mantis Claw to climb up the walls of the arena and staying above them while slashing downwards. As they have no upward attacks, they cannot retaliate while the Knight is still able to deal damage.
Spells help to chip at their health before going for the kill.
Location
This enemy is only found in the Colosseum of Fools, in the last two trials.
References
---

# 文档 [381] Wyrms
- 类别：lore
- 标识：wyrms
- 路径：wiki/Wyrms

# Lore：Wyrms
**Wyrms** were ancient, powerful beings who "pulled bugs into their thrall". They were larger than even Bardoon, though they had fewer limbs. They also had the ability of foresight, meaning that they could predict the future to some extent. One of these Wyrms died in Kingdom's Edge, transforming into the Pale King.
There is a reference to another being called the *Blackwyrm* in White Defender's journal entry. This creature shares the word "wyrm" in its name; however, it is unclear whether it was a living Wyrm, a place or a moniker for something else.
At a certain point, all Wyrms died out or were wiped out from the world of Hallownest.
Cast-Off Shell
The former body of the Pale King, the Cast-Off Shell similarly has a horned crown. The ash falling in Kingdom's Edge is moult that originates from this decaying corpse. At the very end of the Cast-Off Shell, the King's Brand can be acquired by the Knight, marking them as King.
---
